# PLAN_ARCHIVE.md — Completed-milestone history

> Append-only companion to **[`docs/PLAN_SHORT.md`](PLAN_SHORT.md)**. PLAN_SHORT is the
> operational doc read at the start of every session, so it carries **only the current
> milestone**. When a milestone rolls, `/wrap-session` **moves** (never deletes —
> `docs/AGENTS.md` §4/§7) the just-closed milestone's completed-milestone section, its
> Decided entries, and its Done log into this file. **Newest archive batch on top;** within
> a batch the original reverse-chronological order is preserved verbatim. Nothing here is
> live — for open work and the current milestone see `docs/PLAN_SHORT.md`.

---

## Archived 2026-07-23 (Session 101): Graph quality — curate the graph you have (V1 → V2)

Moved out of `docs/PLAN_SHORT.md` at the **Graph-quality → next-milestone roll** (`docs/AGENTS.md` §7; *move, not delete* — §4). Content is verbatim as it stood at the close of Graph quality (Session 100 was the milestone's last build session; Session 101 is the roll itself). The milestone ran **Sessions 68–100** and shipped **S0–S7** — of those 33 sessions, 8 were the milestone's own build slices, 6 were security-treadmill maintenance, and 6 were an owner-directed out-of-sequence tooling-extraction detour. Includes the milestone task section, every Graph-quality Decided + Done entry, the cross-cutting items Graph quality **resolved**, and the Blocked item it resolved (the review-gate policy). Newest batch on top; within each group the original reverse-chronological order is preserved.

**Not moved here:** the six cross-cutting items still **live** (they stay in `PLAN_SHORT.md` regardless of which milestone raised them — §7 "what never moves"), and the ten items that aged out under the new **two-roll rule**, which went to [`docs/BACKLOG.md`](BACKLOG.md) instead — see that file's *"Aged-out cross-cutting items"* section.

---

**Completed-milestone task section (Graph quality).**

## Completed milestone: Graph quality — curate the graph you have (V1 → V2)

**Goal:** V1 is feature-complete; by design the PoC **over-extracts** — every graph write passes
the human gate (INV-1/INV-9), so the real Oakhaven graph is dense, with duplicates, near-synonym
edges, and spurious nodes *intentionally* left for curation. The owner now has that graph and wants
to **clean it in place** — fluid, context-rich tools to curate the entities and edges that already
exist, rather than re-running or improving extraction. The enabling insight: **the human gate is
only as good as the context it shows you**, and bringing the source text to the decision point is
mostly *cheap* — the data already exists (staged relations carry `paragraph_id`, entities carry
mentions; the write plumbing exists behind the gate with a full undo log). So this milestone is
**largely a UX-surfacing job, not net-new write plumbing.** Improving *extraction* is a later,
separate pass (owner steer, S66). **Source of truth for scope:**
[`docs/specs/graph-quality.md`](specs/graph-quality.md) (owner-approved, S66 prep gate).

**Slicing — RESHAPED 2026-06-26 (Session 69)** after the S0 decompose + owner resolutions (see Decided
below + `architecture/proposals/graph-curation-surface.md`): **navigation pulled early** (you can't curate
a hairball you can't see), **two human-gated "suggest, then you decide" passes added** (duplicate entities
S4, synonymous predicate-names S6), the **predicate work reframed as *naming normalisation*** (not
edge-joining), and the **§4 edge handle reserved**. Each slice is detailed (a branchy one gets a
`meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0) when picked up.

1. [x] **S0 — Decompose the graph-curation surface** *(architecture, no build; ✅ DONE Session 69)*.
   `decompose-requirement` → the `graph-curation-surface` proposal (register **DM-GQ-1..7 / OQ-29 —
   RESOLVED** by owner Session 69). Defining finding: the edit/merge/delete/undo plumbing already ships
   (`EntityEditService`, M4.S3a/S3b) but only on the reader's panel — so the editing slices are
   UX-surfacing onto the canvas. **§4 resolved = reserve a stable edge handle** (ADR at build).
2. [x] **S1 — Stop silent data loss** *(correctness; standalone, cheap; ✅ DONE Session 71, PR #164)*.
   The auto-chunker could drop trailing paragraphs and report success. One canonical range invariant
   (`domain.paragraph_range_problem`: covers every paragraph `[0, count)`, nothing past the end) folded
   into the agent's retried validation via a new `check` hook — so **both** a coverage gap *and* an
   overshoot re-prompt (symmetric recovery, owner option B after `/code-review`) — with the coordinator
   re-asserting it as a terminal `OutlineCoverageError` backstop. Failing tests first; live-verified
   (real auto-chunk + a controlled-provider guard demo). Overlap-rejection deferred to `docs/BACKLOG.md`.
   (OQ-28 hazard #1.)
3. [x] **S2 — Navigate the graph** *(pulled early — the foundation curation sits on; ✅ BUILT Session 73, PR #168)*.
   The §3.4 filters (entity type / story / connection density) + node search by name + **a better layout
   algorithm** to spread a dense graph (today's `cose` is an unnavigable hairball). You can't curate a
   graph you can't see — lands before the curation slices. (Was S4 + the layout dimension, owner S69.)
   **Step-0 decompose ✅ DONE + register RESOLVED (Session 72, PR #166)** — `architecture/proposals/graph-navigation.md`
   (DM-GN-1..4 / OQ-30): client-side filtering (no new backend), `cytoscape-fcose` layout, S2 stays
   navigation-only (edge panel = S3), AND-combine + hide-and-relayout + search-as-focus. **Built Session 73**
   — pure `graphFilters.ts` (type/degree/diacritic-search) + `useDebouncedValue` hook, test-first;
   `cytoscape-fcose` pinned via `/add-dependency`; `/review-pr` + multi-agent `/code-review` folded;
   browser-smoke-verified at Oakhaven scale (186 nodes). Two follow-ups → `docs/BACKLOG.md` (URL-persist
   view state; label crowding on an all-disconnected filtered set).
4. [x] **S3 — Edge evidence + verifiable merges** *(the enabler; decomposed + register RESOLVED Session 74; **S3a BUILT Session 75, PR #172**; **S3b BUILT Session 76, PR #174** — ✅ COMPLETE)*. Click an
   edge → predicate + source sentence(s); each entity-merge option shows a context quote + type +
   aliases; cheap safeguards ride here (gate exact-name duplicate creation; don't present a score-100
   exact-name match as self-evidently correct for common-noun/group types; fix the amber
   "merge target" highlight that makes a *New* card read as a merge). **As decomposed (S74):** a
   read/verify slice (writes nothing) needing new **read** surfaces, not storage — **DM-EE-1** focused
   per-edge BFF evidence read (fetch-on-tap) · **DM-EE-2** all `written` `staged_relations` by `edge_id`
   (+ index; zero-provenance → "added manually") · **DM-EE-3** enrich all merge surfaces
   (type+aliases+quote+`target_canonical_name` — closes the cross-cutting `CandidateView` item below at
   build) · **DM-EE-4** score-trap solved by context not type-classification (INV-4) · **DM-EE-5**
   client-side warn-and-offer dup-create gate · **DM-EE-6** be-first (**S3a**) / fe-second (**S3b**, amber
   fix rides). The §4 edge handle is **not** consumed here (S3 reads by content id; the handle is an
   edge-*write* concern, S5/S6). No spec amendment; no ADR.
   - [x] **S3a — backend read surfaces (BUILT Session 75, PR #172).** `GET …/relations/{edge_id}/evidence`
     (predicate + all `written` `staged_relations` by `edge_id`, batched; zero-provenance → empty) via a new
     `get_written_by_edge_id` + `edge_id` index + pure `domain/edge_evidence.py`; `CandidateView` enriched
     (`target_canonical_name` + typed `AlternativeView` type/aliases/quote, best-effort — a graph-DB outage
     degrades to an unenriched queue). `/review-pr` + multi-agent `/code-review` folded; all green.
   - [x] **S3b — frontend (BUILT Session 76, PR #174).** edge-tap + `EdgeEvidencePanel`; render the merge context
     (**tolerate null type/aliases/quote — the enriched fields degrade to null when the graph DB is down**);
     DM-EE-4 (honest score) + DM-EE-5 (dup-create warn) + the amber "merge target" highlight fix on *New* cards.
     Deferred limitation to note: the evidence read returns **200 + empty** for both a manually-added edge and a
     stale/nonexistent `edge_id` (distinguishing them needs a Neo4j edge-existence check — documented, deferred).
5. [x] **S4 — Suggest duplicate clusters over the accepted graph** *(NEW — proactive entity dedup;
   human-gated; ✅ COMPLETE — S4a be Session 78 / S4b fe Session 79)*. Re-point the §3.3 cascade matcher at the already-accepted entities → surface likely-dup
   clusters the author would otherwise hunt for; the human reviews + commits via the existing merge
   (INV-1/INV-9 hold — *suggests*, never auto-merges). Promoted from `docs/BACKLOG.md` (graph-traversal
   discovery), owner S69. **Step-0 decompose ✅ DONE + register RESOLVED (Session 77)** —
   `architecture/proposals/graph-cluster-dedup.md` (DM-CD-1..6 / OQ-32): **pairwise** suggestions
   (transitive deferred), **eager/recall-first deterministic** matching (name + embeddings, ambiguous
   floor, a `duplicate_suggest_floor` knob), **persist dismissals** (a Postgres pair-store — ADR at build),
   a **dedicated review-queue-like list**, split **S4a** be / **S4b** fe. No net-new graph write; no spec
   amendment at decompose time.
   - [x] **S4a — backend duplicate-suggestion surface (BUILT Session 78, PR #179).** A pure
     `domain/duplicate_clusters.py` self-join (`suggest_duplicate_pairs`, reusing the relocated
     `name_match_score`/`cosine_similarity`) → `GET …/duplicate-suggestions` (assemble snapshot → self-join
     → drop dismissed → enrich with S3 type/aliases/quote → rank), plus the DM-CD-3 dismissal store (new
     staging-side `duplicate_suggestion_dismissals` table + `POST`/`DELETE …/dismiss`, reversible) and a
     `duplicate_suggest_floor` config knob. The pure `cosine_similarity`+`name_match_score` core was
     **relocated into `domain/name_similarity.py`** (owner call) so the pure self-join reuses them without a
     `domain/↛agents/` break. Suggests only — writes no graph (INV-1/INV-9); type soft-only (INV-4);
     zero-vector → name-only. **ADR 0010** records the dismissal store. `/review-pr` + required `/code-review`
     folded (4 findings: offload the O(n²) self-join off the event loop, complete the primitive extraction,
     gather independent reads, drop a speculative column). Live-driven on the real Oakhaven graph.
   - [x] **S4b — the review-list frontend (BUILT Session 79, PR #181).** A dedicated `/stories/:id/duplicates`
     "possible duplicates" list (DM-CD-4): each row = the pair + S3 (DM-EE-3) verification context + honest
     name/embedding score labels + an in-quote **mention highlight** (owner ask) + a Keep/Merge hint; accept
     picks the survivor explicitly (owner call) and feeds the *existing* merge (conflicts resolved by hand);
     dismiss / un-dismiss persist + reverse (DM-CD-3) with a transient Undo. **Folded the cross-cutting
     shared-`useReviewQueue`** — extracted a generic `hooks/useReviewQueue.ts` and migrated *all three* review
     screens onto it (owner call). `/review-pr` + required `/code-review` folded (3 findings). Live-driven on
     the real Oakhaven graph (234 pairs). Two upstream quality findings → `docs/BACKLOG.md` (name-scorer
     over-match; embeddings absent).
6. [x] **S5 — The graph as an in-place editing surface** *(the spine; sliced S5a node / S5b edge per S0; ✅ COMPLETE — S5a Session 81 / S5b-be Session 82 / S5b-fe Session 83)*.
   Bring the existing write paths onto the canvas — edit node name/type/aliases/properties, merge, delete;
   edit / re-target / delete an edge — with the human gate + undo intact (INV-1/INV-9/INV-3). Interaction =
   a selection-driven editable panel (right-click deferred), reusing the reader's edit panel (DM-GQ-3).
   Reserves the **§4 edge handle**.
   **Step-0 decompose ✅ DONE + register RESOLVED (Session 80, PR #183)** — `architecture/proposals/graph-canvas-editing.md`
   (DM-S5-1..6 / OQ-33). **Defining finding (two code surveys):** node-editing already ships end-to-end and is
   wired on the *reader* → **S5a is pure canvas-surfacing**; the only net-new plumbing is **edge-editing**
   (`edit-predicate`/`re-target` have no atomic op — a client remove+add re-keys the content-addressed
   `relation_edge_id`), so **S5b is the first edge-*write* slice and consumes the reserved §4 handle**
   (surrogate key, DM-GQ-1 — confirmed unbuilt; **ADR + the "handle survives curation" invariant draft at
   the S5b build**). **Owner resolutions:** DM-S5-1 = **extract a shared `EntityEditPanel` core** (reader +
   canvas both compose it) · DM-S5-2 = **atomic backend edge-edit op** (preserves the handle) · DM-S5-3 =
   mint-forward/no-backfill + coalesce-on-MERGE + invariant-at-build · DM-S5-4 = **defer right-click** (panel-only)
   · DM-S5-5 = single S5a slice + fold the §4 tag into S5b-be · DM-S5-6 = panel-vanish guard, LWW-at-PoC.
   **Build cut: S5a (fe) → S5b-be (tag + edge ops + ADR + invariant) → S5b-fe.** No spec amendment; no ADR at decompose.
   - [x] **S5a — node curation on the canvas (BUILT Session 81, PR #186).** Extracted a shared
     `EntityEditPanel` core (new `features/entity-panel/`) the reader + canvas both compose (occurrences/
     ego-mini/relations stay reader-only via `renderReadExtras`); pure `entityEditForm` + `useEntityEditForm`
     keep logic out of the component; mounted on the canvas with a toolbar `UndoButton`; deleted the read-only
     `NodeDetailsPanel`. Panel-vanish guard = pure `shouldClearSelection` (holds selection while dirty,
     re-selects the just-edited node, grace ends on user filtering). **Owner "move the helpers too":** relocated
     `MergeControls`/`MergeConflictFields`/`mergeConflicts`/`propertiesEditor`/`formatPropertyValue`/`UndoButton`
     into `features/entity-panel/`. `/review-pr` + required `/code-review` folded — **both caught a wrong-target
     PATCH** (a re-targeted panel with no `key` carried the prior node's drafts → Save PATCHed the wrong
     entity); fixed by keying the panel per entity (+ two symptom fixes). 451 tests green; browser-smoke-verified
     at Oakhaven scale (edit type → recolour + undo).
   - [x] **S5b-be — edge-write backend (BUILT Session 82, PR #188).** The §4 `edge_uid` surrogate handle
     (`uuid4`, Neo4j-property-only — **no DB migration**; mint-forward on every edge writer, no backfill;
     coalesce-on-`MERGE … ON CREATE SET` — no `ON MATCH`; survivor keeps its own handle on a fold) + the atomic
     `retarget_relation` op (pure `domain/relation_rekey.py` mirroring `plan_merge`'s re-point; reuses the merge
     writer's `repoint_relation`/`fold_relation` op-strings so undo already inverts it) + `PATCH …/relations/{edge_id}`
     (OpenAPI + typed-client regen). **ADR 0011** (escalated form — data-model identity boundary) + **INV-10**
     ("an edge's `edge_uid` survives re-point/re-predicate/merge") minted with enforcer + tests; INV-9 grep set
     unchanged (7th witnessed instance). `/review-pr` + **required** `/code-review` (high) folded — the multi-agent
     pass caught a real **data-loss bug the self-review missed**: delete-old-then-create-new lost the edge on a
     mid-failure → **reordered to create-first** (recoverable duplicate, never a missing edge — the DM-S5-2 window
     closed server-side) + 4 more (honest crash-window docstring/ADR, domain blank-predicate guard, stale
     `AddRelationRequest` docstring, skip redundant endpoint reads). 630 tests green; ruff + mypy clean.
   - [x] **S5b-fe — edge affordances on the canvas panel (BUILT Session 83, PR #190).** Extended the
     S3b `EdgeEvidencePanel` read-only → editable, mirroring the S5a node pattern: pure `edgeEditForm`
     (changed-fields-only patch, ≥1-change + non-blank-predicate validation, dirty guard) → thin
     `useEdgeEditForm` → the panel (read-mode Edit/Delete + edit-mode predicate input + endpoint
     re-target via the reused `EntityPicker`). New `useRetargetRelation` drives `PATCH …/relations/
     {edge_id}` (invalidates the story-graph triad); delete reuses `useRemoveRelation`. `GraphViewer`
     resolves the tapped edge + a `nameOf` lookup, keys the panel per edge, **re-points the selection
     on a re-key** (the new content id), and guards the edge selection against the mid-edit
     panel-vanish via the generalized `shouldClearSelection` (DM-S5-6). `/review-pr` + required
     `/code-review` (high) folded — the multi-agent pass caught a fold-notice-suppressed-on-error bug
     + a test-coverage regression; its "invalidate edge-evidence cache" finding was **refuted**
     (verified `retarget_relation` never touches `staged_relations`), the real re-key-orphans-provenance
     limitation → `docs/BACKLOG.md`. Owner-found UX bug fixed (long source paragraphs scroll inside the
     edge + node panels so the curation actions stay reachable). 489 tests green; owner ran the
     Oakhaven smoke (edit an edge → undo → clean). **S5 is COMPLETE.**
7. [x] **S6 — Predicate- AND entity-type-name normalisation + synonym suggestion** *(the reframed
   "consolidate"; naming consistency, not edge-joining)*. Rename a predicate graph-wide to cut synonym noise
   (e.g. `PASSENGER_ON` → `ON_SHIP`), with an NLP/embedding layer that *suggests* synonymous names; identical-
   triple collapses are reported, not the goal. Human-gated; predicates stay free strings (INV-4); carries
   the §4 handle. Promoted from `docs/BACKLOG.md` (predicate proliferation), owner S69. **Scope extended
   to entity *types* (owner, Session 81):** the same casing/synonym spread the owner saw in the live type
   filter (`PERSON`/`Person`, `GROUP`/`group`/`GROUP_OF_PERSONS`, `LOCATION`/`PLACE`/`Place`, `OBJECT`/
   `ARTIFACT`, …) — types are open-world (INV-4), so nothing collapses them automatically. S6 does one
   suggest-then-you-decide normalisation pass over **both** predicate names and entity-type labels (the
   step-0 decompose scopes the shared vs per-surface machinery when S6 is picked up).
   **Step-0 decompose ✅ DONE (Session 90, PR #203) + register RESOLVED (Session 91 — each as proposed)** —
   `architecture/proposals/graph-name-normalisation.md` (DM-NN-1..6 / OQ-34). **Defining finding:** a predicate
   IS the Neo4j relationship type (renaming re-keys every bearing edge — reuse the S5b `plan_relation_rekey`,
   preserve `edge_uid`/INV-10, fold identical triples reported), a type IS a node property (renaming is a bulk
   `SET n.type` — no re-key/handle/collapse) ⇒ **one shared SUGGEST engine + two forked APPLY paths.**
   **Owner resolutions:** DM-NN-1 = shared suggest / forked apply · DM-NN-2 = fuzzy + label-string embeddings,
   recall-first, `name_normalise_suggest_floor` knob · DM-NN-3 = persist dismissals (reuse S4 / ADR 0010) ·
   DM-NN-4 = graph-wide S5b re-key in one grouped op · DM-NN-5 = new bulk `SET n.type` relabel (INV-9 +1 path) ·
   DM-NN-6 = dedicated `/stories/:id/normalise-names` list, both vocabularies together, be-first. **Build cut:
   S6a (backend) → S6b (frontend list).** No spec amendment; no ADR anticipated. **S6a further split by the
   owner into read-first / write-second (Session 92) for reviewability** — the risky graph-write apply ops get
   their own focused `/code-review`.
   - [x] **S6a-1 — backend read/suggest half (BUILT Session 92, PR #207).** Pure two-rung self-join over label
     vocabularies (`domain/label_synonyms.py` — case-/underscore-normalised RapidFuzz + label-string embedding
     cosine, recall-first; JSON-seeded surface-scoped `uuid5` dismissal id) + a sibling `label_pair_dismissals`
     store (ADR 0010's design at label granularity, no fresh ADR) + two Neo4j `DISTINCT`-and-count reads
     (`type(r)` / `e.type`, null-type guarded) + `LabelVocabularyReader` (one-pass encode via a **shared**
     `EmbeddingAgent`, typed against a `LabelEncoder` Protocol) + `GET/POST/DELETE /stories/{id}/label-vocabulary`
     (reads guarded inside the declared-503 `try`; `name_normalise_suggest_floor` knob). OpenAPI + client regen.
     **verify-at-build (DM-NN-2) on the real Oakhaven graph (227 predicates / 45 types):** the embedding rung
     earns its place — it uniquely surfaces `LOCATION`↔`PLACE` (cosine 0.878) fuzzy misses — so embeddings ship.
     Finding: **case-folding is load-bearing, not just the DM-NN-2 fallback** — RapidFuzz `token_set_ratio` is
     case-sensitive (`PERSON`/`Person` → 17), so normalisation is core to the fuzzy rung. `/review-pr` + required
     `/code-review` (high) folded — the multi-agent pass caught a **real dismissal-id `|`-collision bug** the
     self-review missed (free-string labels, unlike S4's UUIDs, can contain the separator) + a concurrent model
     double-load + a duplicate `EmbeddingAgent` instance + a null-type 500. Predicate name-scorer over-match
     (`IN` subset) → `docs/BACKLOG.md` (S6b tuning). 667 backend tests; CI green.
   - [x] **S6a-2 — backend write/apply half (BUILT Session 95, PR #212).** The two graph-write apply ops:
     graph-wide **predicate re-key** (pure `domain/predicate_rename.plan_predicate_rename` drives
     `EntityEditService.rename_predicate` — loop the shipped `plan_relation_rekey` in ONE grouped reversible
     op, preserve each `edge_uid`/INV-10, fold identical triples **counted-and-reported**; reuses
     `create_relation`/`delete_relation` + the `repoint`/`fold` inverses — **no new graph-write symbol**) +
     a **new bulk `SET n.type` type relabel** (`Neo4jRepo.relabel_entity_type` — the **one net-new writer**;
     recorded per node as `edit_fields` so undo reuses `RestoreEntityFields`; INV-9 enumeration + grep-guard
     widened by the one symbol — **8th** witnessed path; INV-10 marked realized-consumer). **One** surface-
     discriminated apply endpoint `POST …/label-vocabulary/rename` (`get_story` inside the declared-503 guard —
     the S82 pattern) + OpenAPI + typed-client regen. Test-first; `/review-pr` + required `/code-review` (high)
     folded — the multi-agent pass caught a real **`from_label`-whitespace-strip bug** the self-review missed
     (a rename could never target a stored label carrying whitespace) + a redundant-guard cleanup; two
     undo-integrity windows (single-valued relabel drift; graph-wide evidence-last) documented as the accepted
     single-author LWW posture (same as merge/delete), not re-architected. 700 backend tests; ruff + mypy
     clean; no spec amendment, no new ADR.
   - [x] **S6b — the `/stories/:id/normalise-names` frontend list (BUILT Session 96, PR #214).** A dedicated
     review screen mirroring the S4b `/duplicates` list: two grouped sections (Predicates / Types) over one
     shared J/K cursor (flat-list `useReviewQueue`), honest `name match · embedding` score labels + per-form
     use-counts, an **arm-then-confirm** graph-wide rename (owner UX call) with `from_label` sent **verbatim**
     (S95 strip-bug guard), and dismiss/un-dismiss with a transient Undo — all over the shipped S6a endpoints,
     no backend change. Three typed hooks + a pure logic module + card/queue, reusing `useReviewQueue`;
     "Normalise names" link added to the graph viewer. `/review-pr` (caught a graph-write cache-invalidation
     gap — a rename dirties the graph/reader/detail caches, not just its list) + required `/code-review` (high,
     caught an empty error banner on a non-`ApiError` failure + stacked status banners + `Surface` hand-typing)
     folded. 532 frontend tests; lint + build clean. **Browser-smoke-confirmed on the real Oakhaven graph**,
     which exposed the predicate name-scorer over-match live (a bare `IN`, name-match 100, grouped with the
     whole `…_IN` family) → split out as **S6c** below (owner: its own backend unit). The `clamp`-across-four-
     review-modules duplication → `docs/BACKLOG.md`.
   - [x] **S6c — predicate/type name-scorer precision tune (BUILT Session 97, PR #216).** Suppressed the
     bare-`IN`-style subset over-match by adding a subset-**INtolerant** `label_match_score` (RapidFuzz
     `token_sort_ratio`) to `domain/name_similarity.py` and routing `suggest_label_synonyms` through it — a
     bare `IN` vs `STORED_IN` drops 100 → ~36 (below the 60 floor) while genuine variants (`STORED_IN`↔
     `STORES_IN` = 89) stay high; the empty-normalising case is guarded to 0.0. **Owner call after a
     blast-radius grep:** the shared `name_match_score` is a *third* consumer — the **live extraction Stage-1
     matcher** (spec §3.3) where subset-tolerance is a *wanted* feature (the honorific `Bronek`↔`Stary Bronek`)
     — not just S4 dedup as the handoff framed, so the fix is at the label layer only, shared primitive
     untouched. Test-first; live-verified on the real Oakhaven graph (227 predicates / 45 types): 13 bare-`IN`
     over-matches → 0; genuine variants preserved. `/review-pr` + required `/code-review` (high, 1 real bug
     folded — the empty-label 100-score regression) folded. `docs/BACKLOG.md` name-scorer item reconciled
     (label side resolved; entity/S4 side stays open). No spec amendment; no ADR.
8. [x] **S7 — Reader as a correction surface for existing entities** *(close the loop; ✅ DONE Session 100, PR #222)*. Verify/fill
   gaps so the reader's click → side panel + right-click correction (mostly built M4.S3c, spec §3.5)
   works against existing entities, so corrections surfaced while *reading* flow back to the graph.
   **Verify-first found no gaps to fill** — the correction surface was already complete *and* already
   project-wide (`EntityPicker` searches every accepted entity, confirmed in the browser by
   re-assigning to `Blackwater Keep`, which exists only in a sibling story). So the slice instead
   closed a **spec drift**: §3.5 promised a tooltip "brief description" no entity has ever carried,
   amended to a graph-derived relation summary. Both ride-alongs shipped.

**Ride-alongs** ✅ both shipped in PR #222: review-queue "X of N remaining" count (`QueueProgress`);
empty-queue → onward navigation along the curation chain (`EmptyQueueNext`), replacing four dead ends.

**The fork (owner decision after the sprint):** with a hand-cleanable graph in place, decide — go
deeper into extraction improvement (the spec §5 deferred work: re-extraction, eval baseline, relation
deep-modelling, predicate auto-suggestion) **or** move on to V2 Editing (PoC spec §4). After
Graph-quality → **V2 Editing** either way.

> **Before the fork: run fresh sample text end-to-end (owner, 2026-07-23, Session 100).** The
> Oakhaven graph has now been hand-curated across S4–S7, so it no longer shows what the *pipeline*
> produces — it shows what the pipeline produced plus a lot of human repair. Before committing to
> either branch of the fork, write **new sample stories/articles** and take them through
> upload → chunk → extract → review → curate **from scratch**, observing what actually needs
> improving rather than inferring it from a graph that has been cleaned. This is the same move that
> earned its keep in Session 33 (the first live end-to-end run surfaced ~12 real gaps and killed the
> auto-commit idea outright) — and the S7 walk is fresh evidence for it, having turned up a 14 s
> stall, a hub-monopolising tooltip, an evidence-free normalise-names card, and a 24 %-isolated
> graph, none of which any green test suite had flagged. Treat the fork as *informed by* that run,
> not decided before it.

- [x] ~~**`CandidateView` carries no merge-*target* name — Stage-2/3 merges show a generic label (Session 25).**~~ ✅ **Resolved 2026-07-01 (Session 75, Graph-quality S3a, PR #172):** `CandidateView` now carries `target_canonical_name` (resolved at read time from the accepted graph), so a non-top-3 merge target shows its real name instead of "an existing entity"; the frontend render lands in S3b. Original context kept below. — The review card resolves the proposed merge target's name by matching `target_entity_id` against the staged top-3 `alternatives` — but those are ranked by **RapidFuzz** while a Stage-2/3 merge target is chosen by **embedding cosine / judge** (`candidate_staging._cascade` + `matching_agent.stage2`), a different signal, so the target need not be in the list. `CandidateView` (`api/stories.py`) exposes only `target_entity_id`, no name, so on those paths the badge falls back to `Merge → an existing entity` (the `/code-review` should-fix; the raw-UUID was folded out in S4b). Proper fix: add `target_canonical_name` to `CandidateView` (resolve it at stage time from the in-scope `existing`/`snapshot` entities, or at read time) so the reviewer sees *what* they're merging into on every path. Backend slice + openapi regen — track here, do when the §3.3 review UX is tightened. **Decided (Graph quality — Sessions 68–100).**

- **2026-07-23 — Session 100 (b): the S7 build + a perf follow-up whose headline fix was REVERTED after review (PRs #222, #223, both squash-merged).** Four decisions worth keeping. **(a) Tooltip ordering = one line per distinct *neighbour*, ranked by the neighbour's distinct-neighbour count.** Two bugs, both found by looking at the real graph rather than fixtures: ordering by degree alone let a single hub occupy all three slots (*"→ HUNTS Locke / ← CAUGHT Locke / ← POINTS_AT Locke"* — one thing said three times), and after collapsing the display, `degree` still counted incident **edges**, so a dead end joined by four parallel edges outranked a genuine hub. `overflow` counts unshown *neighbours*, so "+N more" means "N more connections". *Rejected:* alphabetical and direction-grouped orderings (both pick their three by accident of the alphabet). **(b) The tooltip summary is deliberately PROJECT-scoped** though the §3.4 graph view defaults to `scope=story` (DM-MS-2) — summarising an entity's role across every story is the point of a shared world graph. Raised by `/code-review` as a possible leak, resolved by the owner as intent, and pinned in three homes (spec §3.5, the call site, an integration test) so it doesn't read as an oversight. **(c) The normalise-names refetch was re-classified from "post-PoC polish" to blocking on a measurement** — the owner described it as "takes a moment"; it was a ~14 s request that queued refetches until the browser's ~6 connections per origin were exhausted and every other page starved behind them. Fixed by caching label embeddings by string on the app-lifetime `LabelVocabularyReader` (~14–18 s → ~1.4 s), keyed on the **bare label and shared across projects** (a vector depends only on the string; per-project keys would forfeit the sharing), with an `asyncio.Lock` closing a model double-load race `/code-review` found. **(d) The optimistic row-drop built alongside it was REVERTED before merge** — `/code-review` showed it introduced a worse problem than the latency it removed: `useReviewQueue`'s cursor is a bare index that is only *clamped*, never re-anchored, so dropping a row ~50 ms after the keypress (rather than when the refetch landed 14–18 s later) moved a latent hazard into the middle of rapid keyboard work, where a `J` pressed before the response lands shifts the highlight silently and the next decision is persisted against a pair the author never saw. Verified against the live dismissal log that it had not actually bitten (decisions were 1–8 s apart, far outside the ~50 ms window) and that the blast radius was smaller than first stated: a dismissal is staging-side and reversible (INV-9 holds, no graph write), and renames need two deliberate clicks so were never exposed. Backlogged as one coherent item — *instant repaint needs an identity-anchored cursor first*, a real improvement for all four queues since the same shift-under-the-cursor exists on every refetch today. **Both review gates ran on both PRs; `/code-review` found real bugs `/review-pr` missed on each** (the ranking metric + an inert ordering test; the cursor race + three consequences). **Four backlog items opened from working the real graph:** the normalise-names card shows no evidence behind its labels (the owner hit `LOCATED_IN` vs `PINPOINTED` and could not decide — dumping the bearing edges settled it in seconds, and it is the milestone's own "the gate is only as good as the context it shows you" thesis left unapplied to S6); **24 % of the graph is isolated** (39 of 161 entities, with 68 more at degree 1 — two thirds is degree ≤ 1) with no bulk triage surface; the identity-anchored cursor above; and — recorded at the **fork**, not the backlog — run **fresh sample text end-to-end before choosing** between deeper extraction work and V2, because the Oakhaven graph has been hand-curated across S4–S7 and no longer shows what the pipeline actually produces.

- **2026-07-23 — Session 100: Graph-quality S7 — spec §3.5 AMENDED (the reader tooltip), resolving a drift DM-IH-8 left behind.** The S7 verify-first survey found the §3.5 *correction* surface **already complete and already working against existing entities** — `ReaderContextMenu` offers all three corrections plus re-assign, `ReaderCorrectionPopover` mounts `EntityPicker` which searches **all of the project's** accepted entities (not just those highlighted in this story), and all three routes (`…/tags`, `…/suppressions`, `…/boundaries`) ship. So S7 is **not** a correction-gap fill. What the survey *did* find is a genuine spec-vs-reality drift: **§3.5 promised a tooltip showing "canonical_name + brief description", but no entity carries a `description` anywhere** — `ReaderEntity` is `{entity_id, canonical_name, type, aliases}` and the codebase's only `description` is on `GraphEdit` (the undo label). **The reconciliation sweep found this was already known:** vault decision **DM-IH-8** resolved it 2026-06-18 as "(a) name+type+aliases — the data we have; no new field; a richer description is the side-panel slice's job", and the *code* matches that resolution — **only the spec line was never updated to match it**, and DM-IH-8 explicitly left open "owner may want more in the tooltip — cheap to add under (a)". **Owner's call (plain-language question, three options): derive the description from the graph** — the tooltip gains up to three of the entity's relations rendered `→ PREDICATE Neighbour` / `← PREDICATE Neighbour`, ordered by the **neighbour's connection count** (most-connected first, so hovering surfaces the structurally significant links rather than an alphabetical accident), with a `+N more` line. **Derived at read time, no stored field, no LLM.** *Considered + rejected:* **(i) amend the spec to match the as-built name+type+aliases** (cheapest and honest, but leaves the hover no more useful than it is today); **(ii) add a real authored `description` field** to entities (genuinely valuable — a place to note "the innkeeper's brother, dies in ch. 4" — but a net-new data field touching the graph, edit panel, reader, and OpenAPI: a slice of its own, not an S7 ride-along); **(iii)** alphabetical or direction-grouped ordering of the three relations (predictable but picks its three by accident of the alphabet). This **supersedes DM-IH-8's "defer a richer description"** with a concrete derived one. **Cost: one extra `get_relations(project_id)` query per reader load** — the same read `/graph` already does — plus a pure summariser; no per-entity fetch. **Vault reconciliation routed, not hand-edited:** the remaining homes (`architecture/proposals/m4-inline-highlights.md` DM-IH-8 + its Mermaid + line 52, `architecture/open-questions.md:531`, `architecture/overview.md:110`) are vault files whose only authorized writers are the `meta-architect:*` skills (ADR 0002), so they go to the next `review-architecture` sweep via the cross-cutting item below — the established "route to the sweep" pattern. `docs/PLAN_ARCHIVE.md` is append-only history and stays verbatim.

- **2026-07-23 — Session 99: Cleared BOTH `main` security reds — dropped every OSV waiver via a real fix, and bumped neo4j so six Trivy waivers could be deleted (config-only; PR #220, squash-merged).** A security-treadmill session that opened on a red scheduled `main` run. **(a) Fix, don't extend.** The setuptools waiver's `ignoreUntil = 2026-07-23` expired and re-reddened the gate exactly as S98 designed it to — and this time the drop was unblocked: `torch 2.13.0` (pub 2026-07-08T16:01:59Z) cleared its 14-day soak that morning (verified time-precisely, not by calendar date), so the combined `torch 2.12.0 → 2.13.0` + `setuptools 81.0.0 → 83.0.0` bump landed and cleared GHSA-h35f-9h28-mq5c. **(b) The torch waiver fell out for free** — an OSV query showed 2.13.0 carries *no* known advisory, so GHSA-rrmf-rvhw-rf47's "affects all versions, no fixed version" premise no longer holds; `infra/osv/osv-scanner.toml` now has **zero `[[IgnoredVulns]]`** and the SCA gate runs fully strict. **(c) A second, independent red was hiding behind the first.** Today's run aborted at OSV so Trivy never ran; scanning all gates up front (per `/triage-advisory` step 1) found neo4j red on six fresh HIGHs. Per the combined-gate rule both fixes rode one branch. **(d) Bump the image rather than only waive** — the owner chose `5.26.25 → 5.26.27` (soaked 22 days) on the finding that it ships netty 4.1.135.Final, *fixing* all six netty CVEs waived since 2026-05-21; those waivers were **deleted, not carried**, and a raw pinned-vs-candidate scan diff confirmed no new findings. This finally took the "partial-drop opportunity" the register had noted on 2026-06-19. **(e) The six new HIGHs are genuinely unfixable by any tag** (`.27` and even `.28` lag), so owner-approved §6.7 waivers with per-CVE reachability: three netty bugs are in the **SPDY** codec — a protocol Neo4j does not implement, so the handlers are never in its pipeline; one needs a bzip2 stream Bolt/HTTP never negotiate; the jetty bug is in **Digest** auth (Community uses its own native `NEO4J_AUTH` basic realm); the jackson-core bug needs untrusted JSON (Neo4j's only client is the backend, over binary Bolt). *Considered + rejected:* waiving the six **without** the image bump (would have left 12 accepted advisories, six of which a soaked tag already fixed — a "prefer fix over waiver" violation). All waiver homes mirrored and verified by script; full CI green including all three Trivy steps (no sequential-unmask surprise); `/review-pr` clean, no `/code-review` (zero production code). **Retro (owner ran `/retro`):** found that condition-based *image* waivers had **no working check at all** — both `/resume-session` §3b and `/triage-advisory` step 3 said to re-check them "by running the gates", but that scans the *pinned* tag, which carries its CVE forever, so the drop-condition was **structurally undetectable** (this is why six netty CVEs sat waived three weeks past their fix). Fixed both skills: `/triage-advisory` now scans the **newest soaked tag** with the concrete commands, and `/resume-session` §3b gained a ~2-second tag-freshness check. **Its first run immediately flagged two more stale pins — pgvector `0.8.2` vs a soaked `0.8.5`, and ollama `0.24.0` vs a soaked `0.30.2` — now tracked in cross-cutting.** **S7 untouched — a fresh conversation.**

- **2026-07-21 — Session 98: Cleared a fresh security-gate red on `main` — setuptools OSV waiver EXTENDED + unmasked ollama x/image HIGHs waived (combined-gate; config-only; PR #218, squash-merged).** A pre-S7 security-treadmill session: `/resume-session` §3b flagged the setuptools OSV waiver as past its 2026-07-19 floor (the scheduled `main` run had re-reddened on it). **The intended *drop* turned out blocked**, and the session's decisions were the workarounds: **(a) extend, don't drop** — the fix `setuptools==83.0.0` (soaked) is forbidden by `torch==2.12.0`'s `setuptools<82` cap (`uv lock` fails); only torch 2.13.0 relaxes it (`setuptools>=77.0.3`), and 2.13.0 (pub 2026-07-08) doesn't soak until 2026-07-23. So `ignoreUntil` → **2026-07-23** with the drop-when rewritten to the combined `torch → 2.13.0` + `setuptools==83.0.0` bump. *Considered + rejected:* **bump torch young now (12/14 days)** — the owner initially picked it, but it can't green CI: `check_dependency_age.py` has no per-dep exception, so a sub-soak bump only swaps the OSV red for an age red (retracted after that check; drove the retro below). **(b) Waive the unmasked ollama x/image HIGHs** — fixing the OSV red let the sequential `security` job (OSV before Trivy) reach the ollama scan for the first time in days, surfacing 2 fresh `golang.org/x/image` TIFF-decoder DoS HIGHs (CVE-2026-46602/46604) compiled into `ollama/ollama:0.24.0`. Per the "two unrelated reds on the same required gate combine" rule they rode the *same* branch; **owner-approved HIGH §6.7 waiver** on the established wave-1–6 unreachability (crafted-TIFF-to-multimodal only; 127.0.0.1 single trusted user), condition-based drop when a rebuilt ollama ships x/image ≥0.43.0. - **2026-07-15 — Session 93: The `dev-rituals` copy-model is wrong — future tooling work is a *generator*, not a plugin that owns the skills (backlog note, docs-only).** Using the shipped `dev-rituals` plugin (extraction closed S89) revealed its distribution model defeats the one property that makes the SF skillset valuable — **self-improvement in a loop**: the plugin ships the rituals as *plugin-owned* skills, so in a target repo the skill bodies are effectively read-only and `/retro` can't rewrite them in place the way it does in SF (where the skills are the repo's own files with their own git history). **The reframe:** flip the tool from a *container of skills* to a *generator* — it ingests the reference skillset (SF's `.claude/skills/` + `CLAUDE.md` doctrine), analyses the target repo, and **scaffolds native, repo-owned skills into that repo's `.claude/skills/`**, so they become the repo's own files that `/retro` can evolve. Shape ≈ `meta-architect:initialize-project-architecture` (one-shot, human-in-the-loop, idempotent scaffold), superseding/reframing today's `review-and-integrate` (which wires the *plugin in*; this writes skills *out*). Lives in the `claude-dev-tooling` monorepo, **after the current Graph-quality plan**. *Key insight:* "self-improving, working in loops" is a property of *where the files live*, not a bolt-on feature — that's the whole argument for the rewrite. Logged to [`docs/BACKLOG.md`](BACKLOG.md) under the tooling-extraction item. No spec/plan impact; the current milestone is untouched. (Owner ask.)
- **2026-07-13 — Session 92: Graph-quality S6a-1 BUILT — name-normalisation backend, read/suggest half (PR #207, squash-merged).** First build unit after the S6 register resolved. **Owner split S6a into read-first / write-second** (a plan-mode call) so the risky graph-write apply ops (S6a-2) get their own focused `/code-review`; *rejected:* one big S6a backend PR spanning read/suggest + two graph-write ops. (2) **verify-at-build kept embeddings** — on the real Oakhaven graph (227 predicates / 45 types) the embedding rung uniquely surfaces `LOCATION`↔`PLACE` (cosine 0.878) fuzzy misses, so it ships (no demote); *rejected:* fuzzy-only fallback. (3) the reader types its encoder against a `LabelEncoder` **Protocol** (not a concrete `EmbeddingAgent` import) so the adapter stays free of an `agents/` import *and* tests inject a fake encoder. **Reviews:** `/review-pr` (folded a single-use-helper inline + a missing reader test) + required multi-agent `/code-review` (high) — the latter **caught a real dismissal-id `|`-collision bug the self-review missed** (free-string labels can contain the `\|` separator S4's UUID-keyed version couldn't → `{"a\|b","c"}` and `{"a","b\|c"}` collided; fixed with a JSON-array `uuid5` seed), plus a concurrent model double-load, a duplicate `EmbeddingAgent` instance, and a null-type 500 — all folded; the 5th finding (self-join shares the loop/qualify/sort *shape* with `duplicate_clusters.py`) **deferred at n=2 per the rule-of-three**. **Retro (owner ran full `/retro`):** hardened the `|`-collision lesson into `/review-pr` §1 — the "Shared-helper reuse" bullet now names the *copy-a-derivation-across-a-type-boundary* variant (UUID→free-string → re-check delimiter/escaping). Deferred: the predicate name-scorer over-match (`IN` subset-matches every `…_IN`) → `docs/BACKLOG.md` (S6b tuning, same family as the S4 name-scorer item). **No spec amendment, no ADR** (as anticipated). **Next: S6a-2 (the two graph-write apply ops) — a fresh conversation, test-first.**

- **2026-07-13 — Session 87: tooling-extraction BUILD slice 3 — the keystone `review-and-integrate` skill (monorepo PR #2, squash-merged).** Executed §9.3 of the approved design note: built `dev-rituals/skills/review-and-integrate/SKILL.md` — **the genuinely-new piece of the whole extraction** (everything before was extraction + genericizing). It surveys a target repo and threads the tooling in *deliberately, not blindly* — the analog, for the whole ritual stack, of what `meta-architect:initialize-project-architecture` does for the architecture vault. **Modelled on that skill** (reuse-before-building, §6): scan (stack/CI/docs/deps/images/scanners/tests) → map each ritual to a **recommend/offer/skip** fit → owner selects the active set → confirm → wire in (write `.claude/dev-rituals.config.json`, enable the chosen plugins in `.claude/settings.json`, drop a doctrine snippet into `CLAUDE.md`) → human-in-the-loop throughout; idempotent on re-run. **The two "surface as you build" items, now resolved:** (a) **the `CLAUDE.md` doctrine snippet** = a template that lists *only the enabled rituals* + a one-line when-to-run per ritual (step 4c), so future agents invoke exactly the active set; (b) **fit-detection signals** = a scan→fit table (step 2) — pinned dependency manifests → `add-dependency`, Docker images → `pin-image`, a CI security scanner (OSV/Trivy/npm-audit) → `triage-advisory`, a spec/plan → `review-pr`'s full lens (else it degrades, D3), plan files → the session loop, architecture near-always. **Design nuance the survey surfaced and the skill encodes:** Claude Code enables/disables a *plugin* as a whole (no per-skill toggle), so a repo's **active ritual set is scoped by the config + the `CLAUDE.md` snippet** (which *name* the live rituals), not by flipping switches; skills whose gates are absent **degrade to no-ops** (security skills with no scanner, `review-pr` with no spec). **Both README seams wired** (§8): (1) this skill **owns the config writer** (`.claude/dev-rituals.config.json`); (2) when a repo takes **both** `meta-architect` and the session loop, they enable *together* so the architecture-report **producer/consumer pair closes** — `resume-session §3c` (consumer) triages what `wrap-session §5c`-style roll sweeps (producer) generate — and the skill sets `docs.architectureReportDir`; if meta-architect is taken *without* the session loop, the skill flags that its reports would have no in-repo consumer. **Docs:** added the `review-and-integrate` row to the `dev-rituals` README table and dropped the "coming next / planned" wording from the README + the config example now that it ships. **Review:** the `/review-pr` *skill* is scoped to SF's own working tree (it git-diffs against SF `main`), so it can't target the monorepo diff — applied its **lens manually** (config keys all exist in the example schema; handoff markers match `resume-session` verbatim; plugin-enable refs match the marketplace name; `§3c`/`§5c` cross-refs resolve; JSON re-validated; 708-char frontmatter description); a Markdown skill is not correctness-bearing runtime code, so `/code-review` is not the required gate (consistent with slices 1–2). **Path A held** — SF's `.claude/skills/` untouched; no SF production code (SF green-state N/A). *Considered + rejected:* inventing the skill from scratch (design §6 mandates modelling it on `initialize-project-architecture`); per-skill plugin toggles for selectivity (Claude Code has no such mechanism — selectivity is config + snippet). Remaining: slice 4 (trial-install acceptance test into an older repo), slice 5 (shrunk SF reconcile), then back to Graph-quality S6.

- **2026-07-10 — Session 83: Graph-quality S5b-fe built + merged — S5 COMPLETE (production code, PR #190).** Brought the three edge affordances onto the canvas edge panel (re-predicate / re-target / delete), mirroring the S5a node pattern. **Decisions:** (a) **Extend `EdgeEvidencePanel` in place** (read-only → editable) rather than fork an `EdgeEditPanel` — the edge panel is canvas-only (no reader twin), so a single component with a read/edit split (mirroring `EntityEditPanel`) is simpler than the renderReadExtras indirection. (c) **Re-key re-points the selection** — a content-addressed edge changes id on save, so `onEdited(newEdgeId, merged)` re-points `selectedEdgeId` and the DM-S5-6 guard holds it through the refetch; the guard's `shouldClearSelection` was **generalized** (`selectedNodeId` → `selectedId`) to serve node *and* edge honestly. (d) **Fold note threaded via a GraphViewer flag** onto the re-pointed panel (the panel remounts on the new id, so the note can't live in the mutation result). (e) **Endpoint re-target reuses the existing `EntityPicker`** (the reader's add-relation pick/change UI). **Reviewed** with `/review-pr` + the required multi-agent `/code-review` (high) — the second gate caught a **fold-notice suppressed when the survivor's evidence read errors** (hoisted the note to render in loading/error/populated) + a **test-coverage regression** (the panel-test rewrite dropped two S3b read assertions — restored). Its **"retarget must invalidate the edge-evidence cache" finding was refuted** on verification: `retarget_relation` never touches `staged_relations` (`agents/entity_edit.py`) and `relation_rekey.py` is pure Neo4j planning, so a fold does not merge provenance into the survivor and no cache is dirtied; the real underlying limitation (a re-key **orphans** the displayed provenance because `staged_relations` isn't re-keyed) → `docs/BACKLOG.md`. **Owner-found UX bug fixed before merge:** long source paragraphs pushed the curation buttons off-screen — the edge panel's source region now scrolls internally (actions pinned visible), and the shared `EntityEditPanel` got `overflow-y-auto`+`min-h-0` (active on the canvas, a no-op inside the reader's own scroll wrapper). *Considered & rejected:* pinning the node-panel actions via a flex-1 region (risked the reader's indefinite-height layout — the whole-panel scroll is provably safe there). 489 tests green; owner ran the Oakhaven smoke (edit an edge → undo → clean). **Retro (owner-approved):** added a **`/review-pr` §6 lens** — when a PR rewrites/extends an existing test file, diff old vs new assertions so an extension can't silently drop inherited coverage (the self-review missed exactly this; `/code-review` caught it). **Next: a tooling-extraction unit** (extract the `meta-architect` plugin + the reusable rituals as portable tooling for the owner's other repos — owner directive; see the handoff + `docs/BACKLOG.md`), then back to Graph-quality **S6**.
- **2026-07-10 — Session 82: Graph-quality S5b-be built + merged (production code, PR #188).** The edge-write backend — the §4 `edge_uid` surrogate handle + the atomic `retarget_relation` (edit-predicate / re-target) op, test-first. **Defining shape:** `edge_uid` lives **only** on the Neo4j edge + the `GraphRelation` model + the `graph_edits` before-image, so — the finding that removed a whole chunk of planned work — **no Alembic migration** (`staged_relations` is content-`edge_id`-keyed, untouched). **Decisions:** (a) **coalesce via `MERGE … ON CREATE SET` with no `ON MATCH`** — the ON-CREATE-only semantics *are* the coalesce rule (a MERGE-match sets nothing → an existing handle is never overwritten, a legacy edge stays handle-less); *rejected:* an explicit `ON MATCH SET … coalesce(...)` (a creeping back-fill, redundant). (b) **mint-forward on every edge writer, no back-fill** — the human-gated relation-decide commit, `add_relation`, and the re-key all stamp a `uuid4`; legacy edges get one lazily when first curated. (c) **reuse the merge writer's `repoint_relation`/`fold_relation` op-strings** rather than mint re-key-specific ones — same delete-old+create-new shape, so `graph_undo.invert_operation` reverses it with no new arm (the audit `description` distinguishes intent); *rejected:* parallel op-kinds (duplicate invert logic for no gain). (d) **ADR 0011** (escalated form — crosses the data-model identity boundary) + **INV-10** ("an edge's `edge_uid` survives re-point/re-predicate/merge") minted with enforcer + tests; INV-9 grep set **unchanged** (7th witnessed instance — reuses `create`/`delete_relation`). **Reviewed** with `/review-pr` **and** the required multi-agent `/code-review` (high) — the multi-agent pass caught a real **data-loss bug the self-review missed** (and had *reasoned past*, mirroring merge's ordering): the re-key did **delete-old then create-new** as two Neo4j transactions, so a store failure between them lost the edge entirely → **reordered to create-new-first** (a mid-failure now leaves a recoverable duplicate, never a missing edge — the DM-S5-2 no-edge window finally closed server-side; *considered:* a single-transaction adapter method, rejected as more surface for the same end-state). Four more findings folded (honest crash-window docstring + ADR; a domain blank-predicate guard in `plan_relation_rekey` closing an `add_relation`/re-key asymmetry `model_copy` opened; the stale `AddRelationRequest` docstring; skip redundant endpoint reads on a re-predicate). One deferred: extract the shared predicate validator (finding 6 — rule-of-three, n=2; the domain guard backstops the blank case). 630 tests green (pure planner → real-Neo4j round-trip + coalesce → service-with-fakes + undo → real-store E2E → API contract); ruff + mypy clean; CI green. **Two follow-ups tracked:** the `get_story`-outside-the-503-guard systemic gap → cross-cutting; `merge_entities`' edge re-point shares the same (now-fixed-in-retarget) delete-first data-loss window → `docs/BACKLOG.md`. **Retro:** skipped (owner) — the reflection confirmed the required-`/code-review` rule earned its keep again (caught a real bug the self-pass missed); nothing cleared the bar for a rule change. **Next: S5b-fe** (the canvas edge affordances — edit-predicate / re-target / delete on the panel).

(e) **ADR 0010** drafted (owner-confirmed) for the DM-CD-3 dismissal store — staging-side (INV-9), `uuid5`-PK idempotency idiom, none-at-PoC retention, reversible. **Reviewed** with `/review-pr` (folded a misleading `__all__` + the missing ADR-registry row) **and** the required multi-agent `/code-review` (4 findings, all folded — the O(n²) self-join offloaded via `asyncio.to_thread` so it can't block the event loop; `stage1` routed through the extracted `name_match_score` to *complete* the primitive extraction; the two independent reads `asyncio.gather`ed; the speculative column cut). Live-driven on the real Oakhaven graph (113 entities → 234 suggestions; caught the `Elara`/`Elira` typo-dupe; dismiss/un-dismiss round-trip clean). **Process (retro, owner-approved):** the incomplete-extraction miss (relocated a primitive to be its "single home" but left `stage1` inlined — `/code-review` caught it, `/review-pr` didn't) hardened into a new **`/review-pr` §1 "complete-the-extraction sweep" lens** (when a PR extracts a primitive to one home, grep the module for every inline copy and confirm all were routed through it). **Next: S4b** (the review-list frontend feeding the existing merge).
- **2026-07-06 — Session 77: Graph-quality S4 (Suggest duplicate clusters) decomposed + register RESOLVED (architecture/planning; no production code).** Ran `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` on the branchy S4 slice → `architecture/proposals/graph-cluster-dedup.md` (register DM-CD-1..6 / OQ-32); the owner resolved it the same session, one question at a time. **Defining finding (grounded by the reuse survey):** S4 is **not new machinery** — both the matcher (`MatchingAgent` + `AcceptedEntityReader.load_accepted`, which already assembles the accepted entities' names+aliases+mention-vectors; `_rank`/`cosine_similarity` pure & CI-tested) *and* the merge commit path (`plan_merge` → `EntityEditService.merge_entities` → `POST …/entities/{id}/merge`) already ship. So S4 **re-points the matcher inward** (a *self-join*: each accepted entity scored against the others) to *suggest* likely-duplicate entities, and feeds each into the **existing** merge — **it suggests, never auto-merges** (INV-1/INV-9 hold; no egress/LLM; INV-4 keeps type a soft ranking signal, never a hard filter). Only net-new logic: a small pure `domain/duplicate_clusters.py` (the `entity_merge.py` analogue) + a read endpoint + a dismissal store. The entity twin of S6's predicate-name suggest. **Decisions (owner):** (a) **DM-CD-1 = pairwise for V1** — flat A–B pairs, ranked; the merge is pairwise anyway and this sidesteps *cluster drift* (chaining A≈B≈C when A≉C); transitive `connected-components` (star-guarded) is a **named later refinement**, not a gap. *Rejected:* transitive-now, guarded-clusters-now. (b) **DM-CD-2 = eager / recall-first** — Stage 1 name **+** Stage 2 embeddings, floored at the **ambiguous** band (nothing auto-merges → surface the diminutive/inflection zone; a false positive costs one dismiss click, a miss stays hidden), ranked, **deterministic-only** (no live judge), a `duplicate_suggest_floor` config knob; *rejected:* high-precision auto-merge-bar floor, name-only. (c) **DM-CD-3 = persist dismissals** — record a "not a duplicate" in a small Postgres pair-store (staging-side — INV-9 holds; none-at-PoC retention per OQ-4; reversible un-dismiss), the M3 rejected-candidate-memory (DM-rej) precedent; **ADR-worthy → drafts at the S4a build**; *rejected:* ephemeral (a dismissed pair recurs every open), materialize the full suggestion queue (heavier, buys little — the compute is cheap). (d) **DM-CD-4 = a dedicated review-queue-like list** — each row = the pair + the S3 (DM-EE-3) verification context (type, aliases, quote) + accept→merge / dismiss, reusing the review-queue pattern; canvas-annotation overlay → `docs/BACKLOG.md`. (e) **DM-CD-5/6 = S4a backend (pure self-join + `GET …/duplicate-suggestions` + the dismissal store/endpoint) / S4b frontend (the list feeding the existing merge); reuse the merge unchanged; project-scoped.** **No `graph-quality.md` §3 S4 amendment at decompose time** — the dismissal store is staging-side plumbing, not a change to what §3 S4 already scopes ("suggest … the human commits via the existing merge"); confirm by reading §3 S4 at the S4a build (the M4.S3b "delete → §3.5" miscue). Added three glossary terms (`entity-resolution`, `connected-components`, `blocking`; 31→34). Reconciled across `architecture/` (proposal → accepted, OQ-32 struck, INDEX, CHANGELOG, glossary, learning-log) + this plan. **Next: build S4a test-first in a fresh conversation** (pure `domain/duplicate_clusters.py` self-join first, then the read endpoint + dismissal store + OpenAPI regen; `/code-review` is the required gate once real code lands).
- **2026-07-06 — Session 76: Graph-quality S3b built + merged, a security waiver dropped, and the review-gate question settled.** **Decisions:** (a) **`/code-review` is now a REQUIRED second gate for substantive code** (retro, owner-approved) — settles the S51 open question on three sessions of consistent evidence (S73/S75/S76 each caught a real bug the self-`/review-pr` missed); root `AGENTS.md` Merge-flow "Review model" amended; docs/config/mechanical PRs stay `/review-pr`-only. - **2026-07-01 — Session 75: Graph-quality S3a built + a `/review-pr` §4 lens earned (production code, PR #172).** Built the two backend read surfaces the resolved register (DM-EE-1/2/3) scopes, test-first, backend-only. **(1) Edge evidence:** `GET /stories/{id}/relations/{edge_id}/evidence` returns an edge's predicate + all `written` `staged_relations` for the content-addressed `edge_id` (`{paragraph_id, paragraph_text, evidence_quote}`, one-to-many), via a new store method `get_written_by_edge_id` + an `edge_id` index (Alembic) + a pure `domain/edge_evidence.py`; a zero-provenance (manually-added) edge → **200 + empty** (not 404). **(2) Verifiable merges:** `CandidateView` gains `target_canonical_name` + a typed `AlternativeView` (type/aliases/sample quote), batched (no N+1). **Design calls made in-build:** typed `AlternativeView` over the untyped dict (visible in `schema.d.ts` for S3b — but this forced reconciling frontend test fixtures, a `/review-pr` §2 catch); enrichment is **best-effort** — a graph-DB outage (or transient enrichment-read failure) degrades to an *unenriched* queue rather than 503ing the Postgres-backed review (the `/code-review` availability-regression fix). **Reviewed** with `/review-pr` (caught the frontend-fixture break + `docs/code` drift) **and** multi-agent `/code-review` (caught the Neo4j-503 regression + two undeclared-500 contract holes + an N+1 — all folded, with tests). **Retro:** the self-review had dismissed the contract holes as "matches the existing pattern"; that reviewer-discipline miss hardened into a new **`/review-pr` §4 lens** — a route that declares 503 must route *every* store read through the guard (an undeclared 500 breaks the contract; a sibling sharing the gap isn't a clearance). No spec amendment; no ADR. All CI green.
- **2026-07-01 — Session 74: Graph-quality S3 (Edge evidence + verifiable merges) decomposed + register RESOLVED (architecture/planning; no production code).** Ran `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` on the branchy S3 slice → `architecture/proposals/graph-edge-evidence.md` (register DM-EE-1..6 / OQ-31); the owner resolved it the same session, one question at a time. **Defining finding (grounded by two code-survey agents):** S3 is a **read/verify** slice whose data is *real but not on the wire* — edge **provenance** (source paragraph(s) + `evidence_quote`) survives commit in Postgres `staged_relations` (`status='written'`, keyed by the content-addressed `edge_id`) but reaches no client and has **no by-`edge_id` read or index**; `GraphCanvas` taps **nodes only**; the merge surfaces show a bare `(100)` + a generic "an existing entity" (`CandidateView` has no `target_canonical_name`). So S3's real work is a small set of new **read** surfaces, **not** new storage and **not** the §4 write-handle. **S3 writes nothing** — INV-1/3/9 untouched; INV-4 constrains DM-EE-4. **Decisions (owner — every entry on the architect's leaned option a, a coherent "leaner reads, verify by evidence" cut):** (a) **DM-EE-1 = focused per-edge BFF read** `GET …/relations/{edge_id}/evidence` (fetch-on-tap); *considered & rejected:* enrich every `GraphEdge` in the whole-graph payload (inflates a dense-graph download with one-to-many data read on a few edges) — the M4.S2 DM-SP-1 precedent. (b) **DM-EE-2 = all `written` `staged_relations` rows by `edge_id`** (+ an `edge_id` index) — the complete one-to-many source set; a zero-provenance edge (manually-added — no staged row) renders "added manually"; *rejected:* the single Neo4j `source_paragraph_id` (lossy — only the triggering paragraph). No offset-resolved sentences (LLM offsets null). (c) **DM-EE-3 = enrich all merge surfaces** (type + aliases + a sample context quote + `target_canonical_name` on `CandidateView`) — **this closes the cross-cutting `CandidateView`-no-target-name item at the S3a build**. (d) **DM-EE-4 = solve the score-100 trap by context, not type-classification** (honest score label + the DM-EE-3 context); *rejected:* a "group/common-noun" type heuristic — needs a closed enum INV-4 forbids and under-serves the general case. (e) **DM-EE-5 = client-side warn-and-offer** against the loaded alternatives on exact-name create (never a hard block — INV-1); backend exact-name lookup deferred unless the top-3 false-negative bites. (f) **DM-EE-6 = backend-first / frontend-second** — **S3a** the two reads test-first, **S3b** the edge panel + merge-context render + the three safeguards (incl. the amber "merge target" highlight fix on *New* cards). **No spec amendment; no ADR** (S3 reads what §3 S3 already scopes; the §4 handle's ADR stays with the first edge-*write* slice, S5/S6). **Handoff correction:** the Session-73 handoff's "S3 consumes the reserved §4 edge handle for addressing" was drift — code-verified there is no surrogate handle built yet; S3 addresses edges by the existing content-addressed id for a *read* (stable because S3 writes nothing). Added the `provenance` glossary term (30→31). Reconciled across `architecture/` (proposal → accepted, OQ-31 struck, INDEX, CHANGELOG, glossary) + this plan. **Next:** build **S3a** test-first from the pure `staged_relations`-by-`edge_id` read + the enriched `CandidateView` projection.
