## Completed milestone: Milestone 3 — Cascade matching (dedupe) — feature-complete 2026-06-17

_Retained as history — all sessions done (S1–S4f). M3's outcome: the §3.3 four-stage cascade
**dedupes under full human control** — extraction stages candidates, the human-accept paths are the
only graph writers (nodes **and** relation edges), on-accept re-match + manual handpick keep a single
ingest's graph clean. Retired INV-8; landed INV-1's enforcers (nodes + edges) + INV-9. §9 M3's "dedupe
works, I control every decision, the graph is clean" is met for entities and relations._

**Goal:** the §3.3 four-stage cascade so duplicate candidates become **one** entity
under the author's control — *"dedupe works, I control every decision, the graph is
clean"* (§9 M3). Stage 1 RapidFuzz → Stage 2 embedding cosine → Stage 3 LLM
`JudgeAgent` → Stage 4 human review queue. M3 **retires the temporary INV-8** (no
dedupe) and lands **INV-1's** first enforcer (the human gate).

**Design:** framed in the step-0 decompose — `architecture/proposals/m3-cascade-matching.md`
(milestone register **DM1–DM6 + DM7 + DM-rej all resolved** — DM1–DM4 S20, DM6 S19, DM5 S22,
DM7/DM-rej S23) + the S4a backend decompose `architecture/proposals/m3s4a-intercept-write-path.md`
(build register **DM-S4a-1..5 resolved**, S23) + the candidate-lifecycle state machine
(`architecture/state-machines/candidate-lifecycle.md`, finalises to `living` at S4a).
**DM6 decided (2026-06-11): (A) intercept-before-write** — extraction *stages* candidates,
Neo4j is written only on human accept (so M2.S4's CREATE-on-extract path is refactored).
**The DM6 write-path refactor + INV-8 retirement land with M3.S4a** —
when the human-accept path actually exists; INV-8 stays the live contract until then, and
the cascade is built proposal-only/unwired through M3.S2–S3 (no empty-graph window).

**Feature order** (re-sliced 2026-06-11 / S20 — Stage 1 and Stage 2 split into their own
sessions once the embedding stack's cost surfaced; see Decided):

1. **M3.S1 — `MatchingAgent` Stage 1 (RapidFuzz).** ✅ **DONE (PR #56, 2026-06-11).**
   Deterministic token-set ratio vs `canonical_name` + aliases; routes auto-merge /
   ambiguous / new by the §3.3 bands. Carried **DM1** (threshold home → `config.py`) +
   the **§6.7 HF-model channel** amendment. Proposes only; unwired (INV-1 honoured by
   construction, INV-8 untouched). _Was "Stage 1 + Stage 2"; re-sliced._
2. **M3.S2 — `MatchingAgent` Stage 2 (embeddings) + the `pgvector` read-path switch.**
   ✅ **DONE (PR #58, 2026-06-12).** `postgres_repo.py` `NULL AS embedding` → real
   `vector(768)` + `register_vector_async` (centralised in `db.connect`); per-mention
   vectors on `entity_mentions` (migration); Stage 2 = **max** cosine of candidate-context
   vs the entity's mention vectors (strict `>0.85`). Carried **DM2** (model
   `paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2`, 768-dim, pinned by commit SHA via the §6.7
   HF-channel — `scripts/pin_hf_model.py`) + **DM3/DM4** (storage). Added the embedding
   library stack + the **torch OSV waiver**. **Foundation-only** (see Decided): EmbeddingAgent
   built but *not* wired into the live coordinator (mentions written `embedding=None`) — the
   embed-on-extract wiring lands M3.S4 with the cascade. Verify-at-build passed: model loads
   on the CPU host, emits 768 dims.
3. **M3.S3 — `JudgeAgent` Stage 3.** ✅ **DONE (PR #60, 2026-06-15).** LLM-as-judge
   (cloud_free via the router — `weight="medium"`/`task_type="judge"`; DM5 resolved),
   strict-JSON `{match, confidence, reasoning}` (degenerate body fails + retries),
   prompt-injection-safe, full Appendix C.3 field set. `classify_verdict` merges iff
   `match AND confidence > 0.8` (§3.3 amended with the clarifying merge rule). Carried
   the **rule-of-three fold** (`validate_with_retry` + `TaskWeight`/`Router` → `base.py`).
   Proposal-only/unwired; INV-8 untouched.
**M3.S4 was re-sliced 2026-06-15 (S23) into S4a + S4b** — the decompose
(`architecture/proposals/m3s4a-intercept-write-path.md`) showed the backend write-path refactor +
the React review-queue UI are too big for one conversation. The invariant flip is witnessed at the
**backend/API boundary**, so S4a is a coherent green slice (no empty-graph window) and S4b is purely
additive UI. See Decided 2026-06-15.

4. **M3.S4a — intercept-before-write (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #63, 2026-06-15).** New Postgres
   **`candidates`** staging table + the cascade **wired synchronously into the `ExtractionCoordinator`**
   (embed-on-extract → Matching Stage 1/2 → Judge Stage 3, fail-closed) + the human-accept write-path
   as API endpoints (`GET …/candidates` / accept→MERGE-or-CREATE to Neo4j + `entity_mention`(+vector) +
   a `candidate_decisions` evidence row / reject→remembered). **Retired INV-8 → landed INV-1's first
   enforcer + new INV-9** ("no automated stage writes the graph") + **ADR 0004** + finalised the
   candidate-lifecycle note to `living`, test-first — the flip test ("extraction stages, writes **zero**
   Neo4j nodes; the accept endpoint is the only writer") replaced M2.S4's "two identical → two nodes".
   `create_entity` → idempotent MERGE-on-id; accept path status-flip-last + deterministic ids (idempotent
   retries); store-down→503 + Neo4j-lifespan-close cross-cutting folded in. **Relations are staged
   (JSONB) but the edge write + re-point-on-merge is deferred to S4b.** Register DM-S4a-1..5 resolved
   (Decided 2026-06-15).
5. **M3.S4b — review-queue UI Stage 4 (frontend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #65, 2026-06-15).**
   `features/extraction-review/` with keyboard nav (§3.3 *entity* elements: quote ±200 chars,
   NEW-vs-MERGE, reasoning, top-3 alternatives, accept/change-target/create/reject), consuming S4a's
   endpoints. Keyboard scheme = §8.3 J/K/A/N/M/R (the §10 q9 pick). Hooks (`useCandidates`/
   `useReviewCandidate`, generated-client-typed), a pure keyboard reducer, `CandidateCard` +
   `ReviewQueue`, route + graph-viewer link. Browser-verified end-to-end (22 staged → accept/reject →
   21 nodes, queue drained). **Deferred out of S4b (tracked in cross-cutting):** the **decide-relations
   action + relation-write backend**, and the **§3.4 graph story-vs-project scoping**. **INV-2 consent
   gate deferred past M3** — *not* landed here.
6. **M3.S4c — intra-batch dedup: on-accept live re-match (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #67, 2026-06-15).**
   Decompose: `architecture/proposals/m3s4c-intra-batch-rematch.md` (register DM-S4c-1..6 resolved). Each
   human **accept** now re-runs the **deterministic** matcher (Stage 1 RapidFuzz + Stage 2 cosine, reusing
   the candidate's stored `context_embedding` + the mention vector just written; **no LLM**) over still-pending
   candidates against the just-accepted entity; a strong match (Stage 1 `>85%` **or** Stage 2 `cosine >0.85`)
   flips the staged `proposal` `new → merge` (+ target + provenance/alternatives). **Monotone** (only
   `new → merge`) → idempotent; writes **only the `candidates` table** — **INV-1/INV-9 hold** (re-match is the
   first automated *staging-proposal* writer, never the graph). New `agents/candidate_rematch.py`
   (`ReMatchService` reusing the matcher; match signal built from the accept's own data → **zero extra reads**;
   Stage-1-only when a vector is absent) + `postgres_candidate_store.update_proposal` (`status='review-queued'`
   guard) + an optional `rematch` collaborator on `CandidateReviewService.accept`, **fail-closed**
   (`contextlib.suppress` — a re-match failure never rolls back the accept; reject/replay don't fire it).
   Vault folds: `candidate-lifecycle` self-loop + INV-9 graph-vs-staging clarification; **ADR 0005 declined**
   (see Decided). Backend-only (S4b card already renders merges; queue refetches on accept). Spec §3.3 (amended
   S25). `/review-pr` + `/code-review` clean. Full suite 301 green.
7. **M3.S4d — manual handpick (backend entity-search + picker UI).** ✅ **DONE (PR #70, 2026-06-16).**
   `GET /stories/{id}/entities?q=` (**project-scoped** — DM-S4c-5) over Neo4j accepted entities via
   `Neo4jRepo.list_entities`, ranked with the **same RapidFuzz signal the matcher uses** (a shared
   `_rank` core that `top_alternatives` now delegates to) — **no score floor** (the diminutives
   handpick exists to catch score *below* cross-category noise, so reachability wins; the human picks);
   `q` never reaches Cypher (injection-safe). `EntityPicker` + `useEntitySearch` in the review card feed
   the existing `M`/merge-accept path; **last-pick-wins** (picking an alternative clears a handpick).
   **Supersedes** the deferred "arbitrary-entity search merge target" cross-cutting item. §3.4 scoping
   reconciled (both routes project-scoped). `/code-review` caught a handpick-precedence bug (fixed).
8. **M3.S4e — relation-write (backend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #76, 2026-06-16).** Resolves each staged relation's
   surface-form endpoints → committed entity ids and writes graph edges under an **explicit human gate**
   (the §3.3 5th action "decide on relations" — DM-Rel-1, owner S28). Built test-first: new `staged_relations`
   table (status lifecycle + evidence — DM-Rel-4), normalised-exact same-paragraph resolution reading the
   committed id from `candidates` (DM-Rel-2; the create-id derivation promoted to the shared
   `domain.candidates.committed_entity_id` helper), `create_relation` `CREATE` → idempotent **MERGE on
   `uuid5(subject_id, predicate, object_id)`** (DM-Rel-6 — one edge per fact across paragraphs, retry-safe),
   `RelationReviewService` (the only edge writer — **INV-1 broadened to edges**, INV-9 second instance) with
   TOCTOU re-resolve + held/self-loop/ambiguous guards (DM-Rel-7), two `decide-relations` endpoints. **ADR
   0005**; DM-Rel-2/4/5/6/7 confirmed at build as proposed. `/code-review` caught + fixed a real bug: a
   *changed* merge target wasn't persisted on the candidate row, so a relation endpoint resolved to the stale
   target — `set_status` now persists the committed target on merge-accept. Re-point of *written* edges stays
   **M4** (DM-Rel-5); per-mention provenance for triple-deduped edges is a post-PoC follow-up (ADR 0005).
9. **M3.S4f — relation-review UI (frontend).** ✅ **DONE (PR #78, 2026-06-17).** The React "decide on
   relations" surface consuming S4e's endpoints — `useRelations` (`GET …/relations`) + `useDecideRelation`
   (`POST …/relations/{id}/decide`, invalidating the graph only on commit), a pure keyboard reducer (J/K
   nav, **A=commit / R=reject** — a §8.3 subset, owner-confirmed S30), `RelationCard` (surface triple +
   confidence, **surface-strings-v1**, owner-confirmed) + `RelationQueue` (window keyboard, per-card
   in-flight disabling, 409 stale-endpoint surface, graph link), route + graph-viewer "Relations" link.
   Mirrors `features/extraction-review/`. Test-first (reducer strict-TDD + card + container + hook).
   Browser-verified end-to-end (commit wrote a Neo4j edge visible in the graph, reject wrote nothing).
   **`/code-review` (6-finder) caught a real bug `/review-pr` missed:** `decideMessage` mapped 409 →
   "already decided", but the backend's 409 is a *stale/held endpoint* (already-decided is a 200) — and the
   test had *masked* it with a fabricated 409 body; fixed + retested, plus two folded test gaps
   (`useDecideRelation` hook test, graph-viewer relations-link assertion). **This closes M3's feature work
   — the §3.3 cascade + both human gates (entities S4a–S4d, edges S4e–S4f) are complete.**

Each ends green + committed; `/review-pr` (+ `/code-review` for substantive code) → PR
→ squash-merge, per feature.

---

## Completed milestone: Milestone 2 — Basic extraction (closed 2026-06-11, M2.S6 / PR #53)

_Retained as history — all six sessions done. M2's outcome: the extraction pipeline is
visible end-to-end in a browser, **with duplicates** (the no-dedupe INV-8 that M3
lifts)._

**Goal:** turn persisted paragraphs into an entity graph in Neo4j — **without any
dedupe** (every candidate = new entity, per spec §9). End-to-end demonstration of
the agent architecture (PreNER → Extraction → Neo4j write; no Matching/Judge yet —
those are M3), the multi-tier router (cloud_free default, paid cloud configurable,
OpenRouter as meta), and the spec §8.5 agent activity panel + spec §6.6 token /
GPU-time budget visible in the UI.

M2 is split into **6 sessions**, each sized for one Claude Code conversation. Each
ends green (lint/type/tests reported clean) and committed, and leaves a resume
anchor so the next session can pick up by reading this file. Order is by dependency
— do not reorder without updating the handoff block.

---

### Session 1 — PreNERAgent (spaCy, deterministic) `[x]`

_No LLM, no router. Per-paragraph spaCy baseline — spec §7 step 3. The
deterministic-first opener: smallest blast radius, gives M2.S3 a real candidate
set before ExtractionAgent is designed._

- [x] **Deps:** spaCy + `pl_core_news_lg` + `en_core_web_lg` pinned. The model wheels aren't on PyPI, so they became a new §6.7 **direct-URL wheel channel** (GitHub-release wheels, hash-locked in `uv.lock`, soak checked against the asset upload date) rather than going through `/add-dependency`'s PyPI path — spec amended, gate extended. See Decided.
- [x] **Failing test first:** `backend/tests/unit/agents/test_prener_agent.py` (path corrected from the handoff's `backend/tests/…` per `backend/CLAUDE.md` — agent tests live in `tests/unit/agents/`) — PL Appendix B.2 fixture + EN mirror; `PreNERAgent.extract` returns `CandidateSpan`s covering the obvious proper nouns, typed via the spaCy → §3.2 mapping.
- [x] `domain/extraction.py` — `CandidateSpan` (minimal: text, char_start, char_end, spacy_label, mapped_type); no §3.2 full-shape fields.
- [x] `agents/prener_agent.py` — `PreNERAgent.extract(paragraph_text, language)`; lazy per-language model load; PL/EN routing by language (no auto-detect); unsupported language → `ValueError`. Pure `map_spacy_label` + `candidates_from_entities` factored out so the mapping/offset logic is CI-tested without the models.
- [x] Per-paragraph dispatch: candidates returned in-process for the test to assert against (the entity store lands in M2.S4, as planned).

**Done when:** ✅ failing test passes; spaCy + 2 models pinned; PL + EN deterministic fixtures.
**Resume anchor:** ✅ `backend/src/story_forge/agents/prener_agent.py`; `backend/tests/unit/agents/test_prener_agent.py`; spaCy + 2 models (the latter in the optional `models` dependency group) in `backend/pyproject.toml`.

### Session 2 — Paid LLM adapter (OpenRouter) + router + budget tracking `[x]`

_Unlocks every downstream LLM agent. **All in-session decisions now made** (2026-06-02, via the
meta-architect dogfood — see Decided + `docs/decisions/0003` + `architecture/proposals/m2s2-llm-router-budget-cap.md`):
hand-rolled `httpx` adapters (not SDKs); provider order Ollama → OpenRouter → Grok → Anthropic →
Google → OpenAI with **OpenRouter the only paid route built now**; per-day USD cap; control-first
**pause-and-ask** on free-quota-exhaustion or cap (never silent paid escalation)._

- [x] **Grow the seam first:** extend `adapters/llm/base.py` — `CompletionResult` + the `LLMProvider` Protocol carry usage (`model`, `input_tokens`, `output_tokens`, nullable `gpu_seconds`, `cost_estimate`) and the §6.5 `cost_per_1k_tokens` / `rate_limit_kind`; **`adapters/llm/ollama.py` stops discarding** Ollama's `prompt_eval_count`/`eval_count` (INV-5 / OQ-7).
- ~~[ ] `adapters/llm/anthropic.py` — `AnthropicProvider` picked first…~~ **struck 2026-06-02:** not Anthropic-first; direct vendor adapters deferred (OpenRouter covers them). See Decided / ADR 0003.
- ~~[ ] `adapters/llm/openai.py` + `adapters/llm/grok.py` — scaffolded…~~ **struck 2026-06-02:** deferred to "as needed" (was M2.S6 for OpenRouter; vendor stubs no longer scaffolded in S2).
- [x] `adapters/llm/openrouter.py` — `OpenRouterProvider`, hand-rolled `httpx` mirroring `OllamaProvider` (OpenAI-compatible `/chat/completions`, bearer auth, model passthrough, injectable transport). The **first failing test** of the session: this adapter against a mocked transport, asserting the **system-derived usage fields** + a **cap-refusal path** from the start. (Cap-refusal landed as HTTP 402 → `BudgetExceededError`.)
- [x] `adapters/llm/router.py` — `LLMRouter.complete(weight, task_type)` per **amended** §6.5 (orchestrates the call, not `route()→provider` — see Decided): light → cloud_free on a GPU-less host; medium → cloud_free; heavy → cloud_strong preferring OpenRouter. **Error-discriminated** within-tier failover (429/5xx/**transport errors** → fail over; 401 → fail over but not quota; other 4xx → re-raise). Only **pure-429** cloud_free exhaustion → pause-and-ask (`QuotaExhaustedError`); cap → `BudgetExceededError`. Tier/provider/model **system-derived** (INV-7). _Schema-retry stays in the agent (ChunkingAgent pattern), not the router — see Decided._
- [x] Cost tracking per **amended** §6.6: one `llm_calls` Postgres table, one row per call **incl. refusals/failures**; record input/output **tokens whenever the provider returns them** (incl. Ollama's `eval_count`/`prompt_eval_count`), nullable `cost_estimate` (paid), nullable `gpu_seconds` (Ollama Cloud); daily / project / per-task-type aggregation read from it; per-day USD cap (`DAILY_BUDGET_USD`) **checked before dispatch** (fail-closed), bounded one-call overshoot documented.
- [x] Status endpoint surfacing budget + Ollama Cloud GPU-quota state (consumed by the M2.S5 agent activity panel). Declare non-2xx outcomes per `backend/CLAUDE.md` "API routes". **Scoped 2026-06-02 (own-review + Codex):** S2 surfaces budget/spend/remaining-USD + GPU-seconds **consumed** (from the ledger) + per-task-type breakdown. The **remaining** Ollama Cloud GPU-time *quota* (spec §6.5/§6.6 "time remaining" / "remaining session quota") needs Ollama Cloud's account API and lands with the **M2.S5** panel — accepted deferral (see Decided), consistent with ADR 0003's M2.S5 panel scope. The endpoint docstring marks the gap; no fabricated remaining-figure in the meantime.
- [x] **Deferred-egress marker:** a clear in-code note at the paid-egress point that the per-fragment consent UI is M2.S5 (D5 — no sensitive data, documented not gated).
- [x] Tests: `OpenRouterProvider` vs mocked transport (usage parsing); router decision matrix + **failover discrimination** (429 vs 401 vs 5xx **vs transport**); cost recording; cap → pause-and-ask path; end-to-end `OpenRouterProvider`→router→ledger. _**envelope-malformed vs schema-invalid** deferred to M2.S3 — the router meets a real Pydantic schema there; the malformed-`200`-envelope record/failover gap is tracked in cross-cutting._

**Done when:** a routed cloud_strong call (via `OpenRouterProvider`) against a mock returns and records a usage row; the cap path pauses-and-asks; status endpoint exposes the daily total.
**Resume anchor:** `adapters/llm/{openrouter,router}.py` exist; `base.py`/`ollama.py` carry usage; `llm_calls` table + writes; status endpoint live. (Direct vendor adapters intentionally absent.)

### Session 3 — ExtractionAgent `[x]`

_Spec §7 step 4. Cloud_free by default per §6.5 agent table; cloud_strong on hard
cases via the M2.S2 router._

> **Design settled 2026-06-08 — build directly from the accepted `architecture/proposals/m2s3-extraction-agent.md`** (register resolved; no owner-resolution step remains). Key decisions are folded into the tasks below: per-paragraph granularity (D4); single-paragraph agent, resumable batch driver → M2.S4 (D5); **`candidate_name`** surface form, *not* `canonical_name` (D1); typed `ProviderResponseError` for malformed-`200` envelopes (D2/OQ-10); soft-flag `evidence_quote` (G5); known-entities/custom-types as params now / PreNER hints deferred (D3).

- [x] `prompts/extraction.pl.j2` + `prompts/extraction.en.j2` — Appendix C.2 skeleton. **Render structure strictly from the trusted template; never reparse output rendered with user-supplied text** (encoded in `/review-pr` §4 prompt-injection-safety check; the same rule that hardened `ChunkingAgent` in Session 3).
- [x] Pydantic schema: `ExtractionProposal` with `entities: list[EntityCandidate]` + `relations: list[RelationCandidate]`; open-world types per §3.2 (string `type` field — examples constrain but no enum); validators for required fields + **non-empty `candidate_name`** (surface form per D1 — **not** `canonical_name`, which is the resolved bilingual name assigned at M3 merge); **soft-flag `evidence_quote`** (drop the quote if it isn't a whitespace-normalised substring of the paragraph, keep the candidate — G5); dangling relations accepted (M3/human resolves). _Follow-up: blank `subject`/`predicate`/`object` aren't yet rejected — see cross-cutting (external PR-#42 remark)._
- [x] `agents/extraction_agent.py` — load prompt → call **router** (`router.complete(messages, weight="medium", task_type="extraction", json_schema=…)`) → parse + validate → retry on schema violation (mirror `ChunkingAgent` retry shape, including the bias-control of giving up after N retries with a clear error). **Single-paragraph** (D5): the batch loop + pause-and-ask catcher are M2.S4; the agent propagates `Budget/QuotaExhaustedError`, never swallows them.
- [x] **Router OQ-10 (D2):** add a typed `ProviderResponseError` in `adapters/llm/base.py`, raised by adapters on a malformed-`200` envelope (missing fields, unparseable body, **and null `content`** — added in `/code-review` fold), that `router.py` records + fails over like a 5xx — distinct from a schema-invalid body (agent prompt-retry). Add the "envelope-malformed vs schema-invalid" router test.
- [x] Per-paragraph dispatch (D4) with known-entities/custom-types context per spec §7 step 4 ("Here are known entities: {existing}") **as params now** — the real Neo4j read is wired in M2.S4; first end-to-end passes empty lists. ~~**PreNER hints deferred** (parameter wired, unused until an eval — D3).~~ **As-built:** the `prener_hints` param was **dropped** (not wired-unused) per the `/code-review` fold — no speculative dead param; re-add with a concrete type when the eval lands (the D3 intent, minus the dead surface).
- [x] Tests: agent against a mocked **router**; happy path PL + EN; retry-on-malformed-JSON; schema-violation → bounded give-up; **empty-but-valid not retried**; **prompt-injection safety** — paragraphs containing `[ROLE]` markers or fake JSON can't forge structure or merge into a wrong entity. _Plus null-content envelope + grounded/ungrounded `evidence_quote` + direct `extract_json` tests added in the review fold._

**Done when:** ✅ against a mocked router, paragraph → validated entity + relation candidates; retry-on-bad-JSON proven; empty-but-valid not retried; injection-safe; `ProviderResponseError` records+fails-over. **All met; merged PR #42 (134 unit tests).**
**Resume anchor:** `agents/extraction_agent.py`, `prompts/extraction.{pl,en}.j2`, `EntityCandidate`/`RelationCandidate`/`ExtractionProposal` schemas, and `ProviderResponseError` exist.

_Spec §9 M2: "Save entities to Neo4j without cascade (everything = new entity for

Folded the blank `subject`/`predicate`/`object` validator (PR-#42 gap) here.

Extend `EXPECTED_TABLES` in `tests/integration/test_migrations.py` to cover it. ✅ **Session 15:** migration created (`entity_id` no Postgres FK — cross-store, OQ-1); `EXPECTED_TABLES` extended; migration smoke test green. _(The repo insert fn + the write wiring are still Session 16.)_
- [ ] **Embedding read path stays deferred** — paragraphs continue to read `NULL AS embedding`. M3's MatchingAgent Stage 2 will turn it on alongside the entity-embedding writes; flag in code (don't refactor `postgres_repo` here).
- [x] Tests: integration against the neo4j compose service; round-trip read back what was written; `entity_mentions` back-reference holds; verify the no-dedupe property (two identical extractions produce two nodes). ✅ **Session 15:** round-trip + no-dedupe green vs live Neo4j. ✅ **Session 16:** the `entity_mentions` round-trip/cascade tests, the live `ExtractionCoordinator` persistence suite, the pure-mapping + batch-driver unit suites, and the route-contract suite — and the CI neo4j service makes them all **run at the gate**.
- [x] **[Session 16] Add the `neo4j` service to the backend CI job** (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) + update the `integration` marker description (now needs Neo4j too). ✅ Done (PR #48) — backend job green with neo4j+postgres services; the netty/openssl CVE-rot the neo4j scan surfaced was waived (unreachable on loopback).
- [x] **[Session 16] Map router exit exceptions → declared HTTP** on the new write path; fold the ChunkingAgent→502 cross-cutting at the same time. ✅ Done: `ProviderResponseError`/`ExtractionError`/`httpx.HTTPError` → 502; `BudgetExceeded`/`QuotaExhausted` are caught by the driver → **202-paused** (the OQ-2 + owner pause-response decision), not an HTTP error. ChunkingAgent now maps `ProviderResponseError`→`ChunkingError`→502.
- [x] **[Session 16] Resumable batch driver** (OQ-2) — the batch driver (not the agent) catches the router's pause-and-ask and resumes from the last-done graph write. ✅ Done: `ExtractionCoordinator`; checkpoint = a committed `entity_mentions` row, written **last** (after entities + relations) so a relation failure isn't falsely checkpointed (external-review fold).

## Decided — Milestone 3 and earlier

_Reverse-chronological, exactly as moved from `PLAN_SHORT.md`'s Decided section._

- **2026-06-17 — Session 31 (M3→M4 roll, docs/governance — no feature code): M3 closed feature-complete; M4 opened with inline highlights decomposed; a process gap closed so review reports get acted on.** All three roll gates ran. **(1) Architecture re-sync** (`architecture/reports/2026-06-17-architecture-review.md`) — first full sweep since edges + the relation lifecycle landed (S4b–S4f); no blockers; **folded** the one decision-independent drift on sight (a ~5-session-stale `overview.md` as-built block, now "M3 feature-complete"); filed **OQ-20** (the relation lifecycle has a real status machine in code but no state-machine note — the structural gap). **(2) Cross-cutting curation M3→M4** (hand-walked per `docs/CLAUDE.md` §3) — re-titled the list, **graduated §3.4 graph story-vs-project scoping to live M4 work** (multi-story breaks the one-story-per-project assumption), added carry-forwards: DM-Rel-5 written-edge re-point (lands with M4 entity↔entity merge) + OQ-20. **(3) M4 first slice = inline highlights** (owner chose it over multi-story/§3.4 and properties-edit — foundational, low-risk, high portfolio value, unblocks side-panel + annotation). Decomposed → `architecture/proposals/m4-inline-highlights.md` (register **OPEN**, DM-IH-1..8 / OQ-21). **Key finding:** accepted `entity_mentions` carry **null char offsets**, so highlighting is a span-resolution problem (DM-IH-1), not a render of stored spans — a read-only projection (most stations n/a; INV-1/9 untouched). **(4) Retro — the report-forcing-function gap (owner-raised, both-sides change):** a review-architecture report has no forcing function (a decision register blocks the build; a waiver re-reds CI; a report's findings just sit). Closed by a **producer/consumer pairing**: new **`/resume-session` step 3c** (triage the latest report's blocker/risk findings — resolved-or-tracked — mirroring step 3b's waiver scan) ↔ **`meta-architect:review-architecture` step 7** (write findings actionable + mirror to open-questions so they're triage-able); noted in `architecture/AGENTS.md` (incl. that step 3c *reads* a report, it doesn't *run* the architect — ADR 0002 wiring stays deferred). *Considered & rejected:* record-only (the gap nearly bit this very session); a settings.json hook (heavier — resume is already mandatory). **(5) Deferred (owner):** the now-soaked **python-multipart OSV waiver drop** — fix 0.0.31 soaks 2026-06-18, couldn't drop on the 06-17 roll day (13-day-old fix fails the ≥14-day gate); drop on/after 06-18, before the 06-19 `ignoreUntil`. **Checks:** docs/vault only — code gates are no-ops; no deps changed.

- **2026-06-17 — Session 30 (M3.S4f relation-review UI, PR #78 merged): the relation human-gate UI shipped, closing M3's feature work; a frontend↔backend contract-fidelity lesson encoded both sides.** **(1) Confirm-at-build picks (owner, S30):** keyboard **A=commit / R=reject** (reuse the candidate queue's verbs for muscle memory; J/K nav) — a §8.3 *subset*, and the card shows the endpoint's **surface strings (v1)**, not resolved canonical entity names (deferred); *considered & rejected:* a `C=commit` key (diverges from the mirror) and a names lookup (extra surface this session). **No spec amendment** — §8.3 doesn't define a relations scheme and surface strings are §3.3's own wording. **(2) `/code-review` (6-finder) caught a real bug `/review-pr` missed (4th consecutive substantive PR — #36/#60/#63/#78):** `decideMessage` mapped HTTP **409 → "already decided"**, but the decide route returns 409 for a *stale/held endpoint* (`RelationEndpointsUnresolved`) and already-decided is a **200** + `already_decided:true` — and the test had *masked* it with a fabricated 409 body. - **2026-06-16 — Session 29 (M3.S4e relation-write backend, PR #76 merged): graph edges now write under an explicit human gate; INV-1 broadened; a real merge-target bug fixed by `/code-review`.** Built the relation-write backend test-first, resolving the whole DM-Rel register. **(1) DM-Rel-4 = a `staged_relations` table** (owner) — a per-paragraph-occurrence row with a `staged|written|rejected` lifecycle, resolved endpoint ids, and the committed edge id; *considered & rejected:* keeping the inert JSONB blob (can't carry per-relation status/evidence for the explicit gate). - **2026-06-16 — Session 28 (planning/decompose, vault-only): relation-write framed + designed; the central gate decided; a meta-architect skill wording fixed.** No production code. **(1) Framing (owner):** the relation-write work is an **M3 slice** — relations are part of §9 M3's "the graph is clean" (and §3.3 lists "decide on relations" as a Stage-4 human action), *not* an M3→M4 milestone roll (M3's *entity* dedupe is done, S4a–S4d). Concrete must-fix surfaced: `neo4j_repo.create_relation` uses `CREATE`, so a retried accept **doubles** the edge → needs a deterministic id + `MERGE`-on-id (DM-Rel-6). **(3) DM-Rel-1 decided (owner): an EXPLICIT human gate** over relations — the §3.3 5th action ("decide on relations"), *not* auto-write-on-both-endpoints-accepted. *Considered & rejected:* auto-write (lightest, but commits a hallucinated predicate/direction even when both nodes are right — the exact LLM error human-in-the-loop exists to catch); hybrid bulk-confirm (kept as a fallback if the explicit gate proves heavy). Implies broadening INV-1 (or minting INV-10) to put the human gate on edges — framed, decided at build. **(4) Slice (owner): split BACKEND now / UI next** (the proven S4a→S4b cut) — the backend (staged_relations table + resolution + idempotent edge + decide-relations endpoints + the invariant flip) is test-first witnessable at the API boundary; the React relation-review surface follows. *Considered & rejected:* one combined slice (too big for one conversation, the same reason S4 was split). Remaining register **DM-Rel-2/4/5/6/7 carried as proposed, confirm-at-build** (the S4a pattern). **(5) Spec consistency:** §3.3 already lists "decide on relations" as a human action, so the explicit gate is spec-faithful — **no amendment needed now** (a precise-mechanism amendment may ride the build, like S4c amended §3.3). **(6) Retro (1 change, owner ran `/retro`):** the `decompose-requirement` + `review-architecture` skills instructed "read the matching template from `templates/`", but **no `proposal.md`/`review.md` template exists** (only adr/component/state-machine/glossary-term/project + the canonical `vault-note.md`); the section structure already lives in each skill's body. - **2026-06-16 — Session 27 (M3.S4d build + security treadmill): two design calls, a multi-PR security detour, and a retro skill.** **(1) Handpick ranking — no score floor.** The `GET /stories/{id}/entities?q=` search ranks with the matcher's own RapidFuzz (`search_entities` reuses a shared `_rank` that `top_alternatives` now delegates to — behaviour-preserving). The *planned* score floor was **dropped during the build** after measuring: the duplicates handpick exists to catch — "Kasia"↔"Katarzyna" (43), "Bronek"↔"Bronisław" (53) — score *below* unrelated cross-category noise ("Warszawa"↔"Wars" 67), so any floor that cuts noise also hides the target. Resolution: rank, cap at top-N, keep low matches reachable; the human (INV-1) picks. *Considered & rejected:* a floor (re-introduces the matcher's blind spot); substring/Cypher `CONTAINS` (worse for diminutives + would put `q` in Cypher). **(2) Handpick precedence — last-pick-wins.** `mergeTarget = handpicked ?? pickedAlternative` gave the handpick *static* precedence, so after handpicking you couldn't switch back to a top-3 alternative (`/code-review` caught it). Fixed: picking an alternative clears the handpick (+ its active highlight), so the most recent choice wins. **(3) Security treadmill (owner-decided approach).** On opening PR #70, CI surfaced two reds beyond the known vite #68 — a backend **OSV SCA** wave (new advisories against pinned `starlette`/`python-multipart`) and, after fixing it, an **unmasked** Trivy **neo4j** netty HIGH (CVE-2026-50010, sequential-unmask). Owner chose **soaked bumps + fix-first time-boxed waivers**: `starlette` 1.0.1→1.2.0 + `python-multipart` 0.0.27→0.0.30 + `vite` 8.0.10→8.0.16 (all soaked) clear 3 of 4 SCA HIGHs and the vite HIGH; residuals whose fixes are still in soak are waived with `ignoreUntil` + reachability (127.0.0.1 single-user, no public TLS → the DoS/MITM CVEs aren't remotely reachable) + dated drop-when (tracked in cross-cutting). Merged as PRs #72 (SCA + neo4j), #73 (vite); #68/#71 closed. *Considered & rejected:* wait ~11 days for the cleanest fixes to soak (blocks the feature); scope the pre-push age-hook (a non-security micro-opt — the local hook checks pin *age*, not CVEs; CI is the real gate). **(4) Retro — `/triage-advisory` skill + `/resume-session` step 3b.** The genuine security risk surfaced is a **forgotten waiver** (a known-vulnerable dep shipping behind a green board). New `/triage-advisory` skill owns the advisory lifecycle (enumerate gates + waivers → fix-first via `/add-dependency`/`/pin-image`, else time-boxed waiver, **and the drop-revisit** that removes a waiver when its fix lands); `/resume-session` gained a cheap **date-only waiver-expiry scan** (step 3b) so expiring waivers surface at session start, with the `ignoreUntil` CI re-red as backstop. Root `AGENTS.md` security baseline points at it. *Considered & rejected:* a settings.json SessionStart hook (heavier infra; resume is already the mandatory ritual); a new treadmill *rule* (the knowledge already lives in `/review-pr` §5/§8 + the waiver files).

- **2026-06-15 — Session 22 (M3.S3): Stage 3 `JudgeAgent` (LLM-as-judge) shipped + merged (PR #60), proposal-only; DM5 resolved; rule-of-three folded; §3.3 amended.** Test-first. **(1) JudgeAgent** — router-wired like `ExtractionAgent` (`complete(weight="medium", task_type="judge")` → cloud_free per §6.5); strict §3.3 verdict schema `{match: bool, confidence: float∈[0,1], reasoning: non-empty str}` (a parseable-but-degenerate body — out-of-range confidence, blank reasoning — **fails and retries**, never passes); `classify_verdict` proposes a merge **iff `match AND confidence > 0.8`** (strict edge mirrors Stage 1/2; **fail-closed — a confident NO never auto-merges**). Proposal-only/**unwired** — INV-8 still live; the cascade coordinator that maps a `JudgeError` give-up to "uncertain → review queue" lands M3.S4. **(2) DM5 resolved** — judge tier = cloud_free via `weight="medium"`/`task_type="judge"` (spec §6.5-settled; *confirmed*, not re-decided). **(3) §3.3 amended** (stop-and-amend, owner-approved): a Stage-3 merge-rule clarification — `confidence` is the judge's certainty the two are the *same*, so merge needs `match=true AND confidence > 0.8`; the box's "confidence > 0.8 → merge" is the confident-yes shorthand; the cascade stays fail-closed (no automated stage commits). **(4) Prompt fidelity — the multi-agent `/code-review` catch:** the prompt was first built from §3.3 *prose* and silently dropped **Appendix C.3**'s existing-entity `aliases` (the diminutive signal Stage 3 exists to use) + candidate `type`/`properties`; the single `/review-pr` missed it, `/code-review` caught it; folded to match C.3 in full (both PL/EN), with tests asserting every field reaches the model. `match_stage3_confidence` (default 0.8) joined `config.py` **with its reader** (no dead config). **(5) Rule-of-three fold:** `agents/validation.py` `validate_with_retry` — the shared `render → call → validate → retry-on-ValidationError → give-up` loop; `ChunkingAgent` + `ExtractionAgent` refactored onto it (each keeps its own schema/call/error). `TaskWeight` + a `Router` Protocol promoted into `adapters/llm/base.py` from `extraction_agent`'s local mirror. - **2026-06-12 — Session 21 (M3.S2): Stage 2 embedding-cosine matcher + the pgvector foundation shipped (PR #58), foundation-only.** Test-first, decisions DM2/DM3/DM4 (resolved S20) now implemented. **(1) Foundation-only scope (the session's key call):** EmbeddingAgent is built + unit-tested but **not wired into the live extraction coordinator** — mentions are recorded with `embedding=None`, and the embed-on-extract wiring lands **M3.S4** alongside the cascade + the DM6 write-path refactor. *Rationale:* wiring it now would pull the optional ~2 GB torch stack into the live path + CI and add CPU-slow per-mention compute — a behaviour change in a session where INV-8 ("no dedupe / no behaviour change") is still live; it also mirrors the established precedent that the other heavy optional NLP stack (spaCy/PreNER) is built-but-unwired (`extraction_agent.py` passes PreNER hints as empty lists). *Rejected:* wire-now-with-graceful-degradation (adds a conditional heavy dep + a degradation branch to the working M2 extraction path). **(2) Deps:** `pgvector==0.4.2` (core); optional `embeddings` group (`sentence-transformers==5.5.1`, `torch==2.12.0`, `transformers==5.9.0`, `huggingface-hub==1.17.0`), ~2 GB, CI-skippable like the spaCy `models` group. `torch`'s `GHSA-rrmf-rvhw-rf47` (CVE-2025-3000, **MEDIUM CVSS 5.3** — the GHSA DB field says LOW but the scanner buckets it MEDIUM; aligned the docs to what the gate reports) is waived in the scoped `infra/osv/` register: `torch.jit.script` memory corruption, unreachable here (inference-only `encode`), and **no fixed version exists** (affects all ≤2.12.0) — unfixable-by-pin + unreachable, the two conditions a waiver requires. **(3) Model pin (§6.7 HF-channel):** `paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2` pinned by commit SHA `4328cf26…` (commit dated 2025-08-19, soak met) via `scripts/pin_hf_model.py`'s `snapshot_download`; the script imports `MODEL_REPO_ID`/`MODEL_REVISION` from `EmbeddingAgent` so the pin script and runtime loader can't drift. Verify-at-build passed: loads on CPU, emits 768 dims. **(4) Persistence:** `entity_mentions.embedding vector(768)` migration (`down_revision` was the *real* head `2b5e854961e1`, not the handoff's stale `d721987b4168` — the latency migration had moved it); `register_vector_async` centralised in a new `db.connect` helper routed through all three connect sites; reads coerce the returned numpy array → `list[float]` via Pydantic; writes wrap `pgvector.Vector(...)` (the dumper isn't registered for bare lists). **(5) Stage 2:** `MatchingAgent.stage2` = max cosine of a candidate's context vector vs an entity's mention vectors, **strict `>0.85`** (mirrors Stage 1's strict upper edge); `match_stage2_cosine_merge` joined `config.py` with its reader. Pure `cosine_similarity` CI-tested without the model. **(6) Reviews folded:** `/review-pr` caught a flawed `stage2` sentinel (`-1.0` → `float("-inf")`, so an entity at cosine −1.0 is still selected; + regression test); `/code-review` caught a connection leak in `db.connect` (close the conn if `register_vector_async` raises). **Retro:** generalised the `backend/AGENTS.md` detect-secrets note from Alembic-revision-ids-only to **any high-entropy hex literal** (incl. a pinned model/commit SHA, which tripped the hook this session).
- **2026-06-11 — Session 20 (M3.S1): Stage 1 RapidFuzz matcher shipped (PR #56); M3.S1 re-sliced to Stage 1 only; register DM1–DM4 resolved; §6.7 HF-model channel added.** First M3 code, test-first. **(1) Stage 1 `MatchingAgent`** — deterministic RapidFuzz token-set ratio of a candidate surface form vs existing entities' `canonical_name` + aliases, routing to auto-merge-proposed (`>85`) / ambiguous (`60–85` → Stage 2) / new-proposed (`<60`) per §3.3; proposes only (INV-1 honoured by construction; unwired, INV-8 untouched). Pure `classify` band logic CI-tested without RapidFuzz; RapidFuzz imported directly (the deterministic-local-compute exception, like `PreNERAgent`/spaCy). `rapidfuzz==3.14.5` pinned. **(2) DM1** — the §3.3 thresholds get one config home (`config.py`, pydantic-settings, spec defaults, env-overridable, global; only Stage 1's land now, Stage 2/3 join with their readers — no dead config). **(3) DM2/DM3/DM4 resolved:** embedding model `paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2` (768-dim — **verified** SHA `4328cf26…`); per-mention vectors on `entity_mentions`, Stage 2 = **max** cosine; storage co-located with the mention that already keys Neo4j↔Postgres. **(4) §6.7 amended** — a new **HuggingFace-model pinning channel** (pin the model by immutable HF commit-revision SHA via `snapshot_download` in an optional group, library stack as ordinary PyPI pins; soak verified procedurally against the commit date; OSV N/A for weights) — mirrors the spaCy GitHub-wheel channel. Policy defined now; the concrete pin lands M3.S2. **(5) Re-slice (owner):** M3.S1 = **Stage 1 only**; Stage 2 + the DM6 write-path refactor → M3.S2+. *Rationale, from new findings:* `torch` carries a fail-on-any (LOW, `jit.script` unused, no-fix) advisory needing a scoped OSV waiver, the embedding stack is ~2 GB, and the DM6 refactor *retires INV-8* (graph empty until the S3/S4 queue) — bundling would bury a security waiver + a behaviour change in one large diff. *Rejected:* one big M3.S1 PR (as originally planned). **(6) Self-review caught a real bug** — `classify` used `score >= 85` for merge, but §3.3 writes merge as strictly `>85` with 85 in the 60–85 Stage-2 band; fixed to `>` (the more fail-closed branch) + corrected the test that had encoded the wrong boundary. **Retro:** no rule change — the session's friction ("stalling": over-analysis before producing verifiable output) is an application of existing guidance ("when you have enough information to act, act"), not a gap.
- **2026-06-11 — Session 19 (M2→M3 roll gates): M3 cascade decompose step-0 + DM6 decided (intercept-before-write).** Both owed roll gates ran before any M3 code. **(1) Cross-cutting curation** — the list re-scoped M2→M3 by hand (`docs/AGENTS.md` §3); items that bite M3 noted (embedding read path, agent-dup rule-of-three, store-down→503, graph scoping, `last_call()` tiebreaker, §6.5 dropdown); the stale "lands with M2.S5" pointer on store-down re-pointed to M3. **(2) Architecture catch-up** — `meta-architect:review-architecture` (`architecture/reports/2026-06-11-architecture-review.md`: no blockers; headline `risk` = INV-2's consent gate lost its M2.S5 landing target and the M2.S6 smoke fired real paid egress gate-less — accepted at PoC scale, re-pointed to the M3 review-queue UI) + `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0 (`architecture/proposals/m3-cascade-matching.md`, register OPEN; the vault's first state machine `architecture/state-machines/candidate-lifecycle.md`). Vault reflection of the roll decisions folded (OQ-14 dropdown/INV-7, OQ-15 logging/INV-6-vacuity, OQ-16 the M3 register) — discharges the tracked cross-cutting item. **(3) DM6 decided (owner):** the M3 cascade **gates the graph write — (A) intercept-before-write**. Extraction will *stage* candidates (Postgres); Neo4j is written **only** on human accept in the Stage-4 queue. Register items DM1–DM5, DM7, DM-rej stay OPEN (embedding model, vector storage, thresholds home, review-queue UX, rejected-candidate memory).
- **2026-06-11 — M2→M3 roll (thin S6): model-override dropdown deferred; observability-logging need recorded.** Resuming on `main` after Session 17 (M2.S5 merged). **(1) Roll decision (owner):** run a **thin S6** — real-provider smoke + §6.7 key-leak verification + smoke-procedure doc — to close M2, then roll to M3. **(2) The §6.5 "which provider/model for this task" dropdown is deferred — it is a feature, not thin polish.** The §8.5 panel already does the *surfacing* half ("which tier/model ran, and why"); the remaining half is a real **user model-override control + persisted per-task-type preferences**, which collides with INV-7 (routing is currently *system-derived, never caller-asserted* — that near-miss was deliberately closed in M2.S2). Building it needs an INV-7/spec reconciliation ("system-derived *unless* the user explicitly overrides"), router plumbing for the override + its interaction with weight-tiering and failover, and a preferences store. *Owner call: not in a thin session* — no rush given free Ollama Cloud credits cover real runs. **Lands as its own scoped piece** (a `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step-0, alongside or after M3); carried in cross-cutting. *Rejected:* surfacing-only (the panel already covers it — near-zero value); cram-into-thin-S6 (rushes an invariant-touching feature). **(3) Triplet→doublet:** with no direct vendor adapters shipping (OpenRouter is the only paid route — ADR 0003), the real smoke exercises **Ollama Cloud (cloud_free) + OpenRouter free model (cloud_strong)** — both adapters, both tiers; an Anthropic-direct leg can't exist (that adapter intentionally isn't built). **(4) Observability/operational logging recorded as a later need** (`docs/PLAN_LONG.md`): the backend emits no operational logs today, so §6.7 "keys never logged" is currently *vacuous*. - **2026-06-11 — Session 17 (M2.S5 step 0): OQ-9 (latency) resolved → option (a), record `latency_ms`.** The §8.5 panel promises a *latency* column and INV-5 + the m2s2 proposal both said a usage row records latency, but the as-built `llm_calls`/`LlmCallRecord` and spec §6.6's enumeration recorded none — a three-home source-of-truth conflict. **Chosen:** add `latency_ms` (elapsed time around `provider.complete`, system-derived; recorded for every dispatched call, null only for a pre-dispatch budget refusal that never reached a provider — external PR-#51 review fold) — a one-column Alembic migration on `llm_calls` + capture in the router; the §8.5 panel shows it. *Rejected:* option (b) trim the panel/INV-5 to match as-built — the spec §8.5 panel already promises latency, so trimming would shrink a stated portfolio-visible feature to dodge a one-column migration. **Reconciled this pass:** spec §6.6 enumeration amended; `architecture/invariants.md` INV-5 latency caveat + `architecture/open-questions.md` OQ-9 struck-resolved; `architecture/INDEX.md` watch line updated. - **2026-06-10 — Session 16: M2.S4 completed + merged (PR #48); OQ-1/OQ-2 resolved; CVE-rot waived across 3 images; 2 retro rules.** The wiring half, test-first, squash-merged green. **(1) OQ-1 (two-store write consistency) — option (c):** write **Neo4j-then-Postgres** and **accept eventual inconsistency** at PoC (single user, reversible); no reconciliation/outbox. *Rejected:* a startup repair sweep (code for a rare local-crash window) and an outbox (over-engineered for the PoC). **(2) OQ-2 (resumable ingest) — option (a):** the **batch driver** (`ExtractionCoordinator`), not the agent, owns the budget/quota pause-and-ask; the single-paragraph agent keeps *propagating* it (M2.S3 D5). Resume keys off committed `entity_mentions`. *Rejected:* swallow-in-agent (couples batching into the fragment-agnostic agent) and no-recovery/re-upload (throws away a long story's work). **(3) Pause response = HTTP 202 + partial progress, re-POST resumes** (owner) — *not* a 402 error; budget/quota are caught by the driver and never reach the route as an error. Only hard failure (`ProviderResponseError`/`ExtractionError`/`httpx.HTTPError`) → 502. **(4) Checkpoint written last (external-review fold):** the `entity_mentions` row (the resume marker) is written **after** entities **and** relations, so a transient Neo4j relation-write failure can't leave a "done" paragraph with lost relations — the original entities→mention→relations order had that silent-data-loss bug, which is also why a new `/review-pr` "checkpoint-ordering" rule was added. **(5) `extraction_model` default = `gpt-oss:120b-cloud`** (cloud_free, heavier than chunking's 20b — extraction is richer reasoning); tunable via `.env`. **(6) CVE-rot waived, not fixed:** the neo4j CI service brought the security job into focus and the sequential-Trivy scan unmasked the same OpenSSL `PKCS7_verify` UAF (CVE-2026-45447) across neo4j→pgvector→ollama plus 2 new neo4j netty HIGHs — all unreachable on a 127.0.0.1 single-user deployment, all verified against the GitHub Advisory DB / OpenSSL advisory (the netty advisory's *second* vulnerable range was the one covering our 4.1.132 — the first range didn't). Pre-existing infra rot, not M2.S4 code; Issue #22 treadmill. **(7) Retro (2 rules, both approved):** `/review-pr` gained a **checkpoint/resume-marker ordering** check (a marker written mid-sequence lets a later step fail over a "done" record — enumerate *each* inter-write window; the P1 bug *both* my review passes missed and external review caught) and a **multi-range CVE-advisory** check (confirm which of an advisory's several vulnerable ranges your version falls in). *Considered & rejected:* note-only (both trace to concrete this-session misses and generalize).
- **2026-06-09 — Session 15: M2.S4 foundation built (unmerged branch); two latent infra bugs found by running it; 4 retro changes.** A build session; the foundation is on `feat/m2s4-neo4j-writes`, **not merged** (half-feature + the integration test would be dead at the CI gate without a Neo4j service — merging it would read as "covered" when it isn't). **(1) Driver: `neo4j==5.28.4`** — the **5.x LTS** driver line to match the 5.26-community server (same-major = lowest compatibility risk). *Rejected:* the newer 6.x line (targets the 2025.x servers we don't run). **(2) Graph modelling:** `domain/graph.py` `GraphEntity`/`GraphRelation` are the *persisted* shapes, **distinct from the agent's `*Candidate`** (candidate has a surface `candidate_name`, no id/canonical/embedding — the M2→M3 boundary). The adapter uses **`CREATE`, never `MERGE`** (the load-bearing keyword for INV-8 no-dedupe — a `MERGE`-on-name would silently violate it); the open-world relation `type` is **backtick-escaped** when interpolated (Cypher-injection-safe — the analogue of prompt-injection hardening, since the type is LLM-produced); `properties` is stored as a **JSON string** (Neo4j can't hold a nested map), `aliases` as a native list. *Rejected:* a global `MATCH (n) DETACH DELETE n` test cleanup (unsafe on a shared instance) → per-test `project_id` scoping instead. **(3) `entity_mentions` migration:** `paragraph_id` is a real FK (cascades with the tree); **`entity_id` carries NO Postgres FK** — it references a Neo4j node, the OQ-1 cross-store seam; `span_start`/`span_end`/`confidence` nullable (the LLM path yields an evidence quote, not reliable offsets). **(4) Two latent infra bugs, found only by *running* it:** the compose Neo4j had **crash-looped since M0** (`NEO4J_server_metrics_enabled` is Enterprise-only; Community rejects it under strict validation — nothing had ever booted it, since the security job only Trivy-*scans* the image) → removed; and **CI has no Neo4j service** (the plan's claim was false) → deferred to Session 16. **(5) §6.7 Neo4j telemetry:** disabled `client.allow_telemetry` + `dbms.usage_report.enabled`, the two default-on channels, **verified against `SHOW SETTINGS`** on the live 5.26 server rather than guessing the setting names (guessing wrong re-triggers the crash). **(6) Retro (4 changes, all approved):** sharpened **both** `/resume-session` (verify infra *runs* — boot the service / grep `ci.yml` — not just that config exists) **and** `/wrap-session` (don't *write* an unverified infra anchor into the handoff — the authoring-side fix, since both false claims were born there), after the handoff twice asserted false infra state this session; corrected the `backend/CLAUDE.md` `down_revision` pragma note (both revision lines can trip detect-secrets — pragma both); added a `backend/CLAUDE.md` note that a TDD integration test for a new module must import cleanly (or it breaks the fast-tier *collection*, not just the integration run). *Considered & rejected:* note-only on the infra-claim pattern (it recurred **twice this session** — clears the bar easily).
- **2026-06-08 — Session 14: backend SCA gate built + merged (PR #44); client DevSecOps notes folded; retro adds verify-at-build rule.** **(1) Scanner pinned by digest, not an Action (deviation from proposal D6, intent preserved):** `google/osv-scanner-action`'s root `action.yml` is a no-`runs:` metadata stub and its reusable workflows do a PR *diff* scan (misses an advisory already on `main`) or a SARIF-upload recursive scan — neither a scoped fail-on-any lockfile *step*. Built the gate as the **digest-pinned `ghcr.io/google/osv-scanner` container** (`scan source -L uv.lock --config=…`), which is *stronger* than the planned SHA-pin (a tag/digest can't move). - **2026-06-08 — Session 12: M2.S3 design settled + spec §6.5 amended + review-model adapted + CVE wave-4 (PRs #39, #40).** A design/governance session, no production code. **(1) M2.S3 register resolved** (owner walked it after a by-hand `meta-architect:decompose-requirement` step 0 → accepted `architecture/proposals/m2s3-extraction-agent.md`): **per-paragraph** granularity (agent fragment-agnostic; spec §10 Q1 stays open); **single-paragraph agent**, resumable batch driver → M2.S4 (pause-and-ask propagates, never swallowed); **`candidate_name`** surface form, *not* `canonical_name` (D1 — canonical/PL-EN naming is M3); typed **`ProviderResponseError`** for malformed-`200` envelopes (D2/OQ-10 — failover-the-provider, distinct from schema-invalid→retry-the-prompt); **soft-flag `evidence_quote`** (drop quote, keep candidate — *rejected* hard-reject as punishing paraphrase); known-entities/custom-types as params now (Neo4j read wired M2.S4) / **PreNER hints deferred** (no speculative prompt complexity). **(2) Spec §6.5 router contract amended** (stop-and-amend): `route(self, task) -> LLMProvider` → `complete(messages, *, weight, task_type, json_schema=None) -> CompletionResult`; §6.5 + §11 "Failover" split envelope-malformed (→ failover) from schema-invalid (→ agent retry).
