(c) A docs-only PR can still go red on a freshly-disclosed image CVE; the green-main "pre-existing/unrelated/diagnosed" exception + `/pin-image` waiver flow handled it without scope-creep.
- **2026-06-02 — Session 11 complete: M2.S2 built — paid LLM tier + router + cost ledger (PR #36, squash `919f9ce`).** First product code on the M2.S2 decisions (ADR 0003). Shipped, test-first, in 6 commits: **(seam)** `adapters/llm/base.py` grows `Usage` on `CompletionResult` + `cost_per_1k_tokens`/`rate_limit_kind` on the Protocol + `estimate_cost` + the pause-and-ask exceptions (`BudgetExceededError`/`QuotaExhaustedError`); `OllamaProvider` stops discarding token counts (INV-5). **(adapter)** `OpenRouterProvider` — hand-rolled `httpx`, OpenAI-compatible, system-derived usage + USD estimate, HTTP 402→`BudgetExceededError`. **(router)** `LLMRouter.complete(weight, task_type)` — tier selection, error-discriminated failover (429/5xx/**transport**→fail over, 401→fail over but not quota, other 4xx→re-raise, 402→don't escalate), fail-closed `DAILY_BUDGET_USD` gate (free tiers never blocked), pure-429 cloud_free exhaustion→`QuotaExhaustedError`. **(ledger)** `llm_calls` migration + `PostgresCostStore` (one row per call incl. refusals/failures; **commits independently** so a failure row survives a request rollback). **(api)** `GET /llm/status` for the M2.S5 panel. Router wired into an agent in M2.S3 (ExtractionAgent); the cost store is wired now (status endpoint reads it live). **Checks:** 128 backend tests (unit + integration vs real Postgres) + 29 frontend; ruff/format/mypy --strict + eslint/prettier/tsc/vite-build clean; no new deps (hand-rolled httpx). All four CI jobs green pre-merge. **Review:** `/review-pr` (own) found + tracked the malformed-`200`-envelope record/failover gap (deferred to M2.S3); **Codex** caught two real router bugs my pass missed — `httpx.RequestError` (transport) uncaught, and every exhausted `cloud_free` tier mislabelled "quota" regardless of cause — both folded with tests, plus the GPU-quota-remaining→M2.S5 deferral (reconciled in plan + Decided; spec goal judged unchanged) and the `api_key` test-literal binding nit. **Retro (2 changes):** sharpened `backend/AGENTS.md` on `detect-secrets` (credential var name must avoid the keyword; alembic revision ids need `# pragma: allowlist secret` — 3 blocked commits this session), and added a `/review-pr §1` **failover/error-taxonomy** check (enumerate HTTP status families *and* transport/timeout errors; verify the exhaustion branch classifies by actual cause — citing this PR). **Lessons:** (a) error-discrimination code needs the *full* exception taxonomy enumerated — catching `HTTPStatusError` but not `RequestError` drops every network failure, and "all failed → quota exhausted" is dishonest when the cause was a bad key; both shipped and both were review-caught, now a written `/review-pr` check. (b) recording a *failure* must outlive the request that fails — the cost store commits on its own connection. (c) `detect-secrets` foot-guns (keyword-in-var-name, alembic hex ids) are now documented so the next migration/adapter-test doesn't re-discover them.

(b) a "test that runs only in CI when a 950 MB model is present" is no CI test at all; factoring a pure seam restored coverage. (c) gating on the right timestamp matters — tag-publish ≠ asset-upload, and uv locks the asset. (d) the retro itself was nearly skipped — folding the user's explicit doc directive felt like "the retro" but isn't; the reflective pass (now enforced in `/wrap-session` step 2) is what surfaces recurring friction like the cwd-invocation foot-gun, which had survived since Session 3.

Own `/review-pr` then surfaced lock-during-LLM, missing `outline_to_tree` unit test, `Literal`-vs-`str` on the response, the `OutlineProposer` `Protocol` (removed 11 `# type: ignore[arg-type]`), and the comment self-referencing the review — all folded. **Process (retro):** two `/review-pr` amendments — added a "dispatch-level confusion in nested structures" bullet to §1 (with the hybrid bug as the memorable example), and clarified §3 Simplicity to say an abstraction that net-removes existing debt is a refactor, not speculation. **Lesson:** Codex caught the hybrid bug class my first review missed, and my `/review-pr` ran *after* the fold so it couldn't be evaluated for independence — running it without reading Codex's notes first is the bias-control I want next session.
- **2026-05-22 — Session 3 complete: LLM provider abstraction + ChunkingAgent (PR #10, squash `ef4a07a`).** Shipped the agent-orchestration spine (spec §6.5) and the first agent end-to-end against a mocked provider. `adapters/llm/base.py` — `LLMProvider` Protocol + `Message`/`CompletionResult`/`ModelTier` (scoped to `complete()`; cost/rate-limit metadata deferred to the router/budget work that will consume them). `adapters/llm/ollama.py` — `OllamaProvider`, one adapter for both the local-small and cloud-free tiers (host/key swap), Ollama `/api/chat`, JSON-Schema `format`. `prompts/` — Jinja2 loader that splits the *template source* on `[ROLE]` markers then renders each segment (so untrusted story text can't forge turns) + `chunking.{en,pl}.j2` (Appendix C.1). `agents/chunking_agent.py` — `ChunkingProposal` schema (with an ordered/non-negative `paragraph_range` validator), `select_chunking_tier`, and the agent (load → call → parse + validate → retry on bad JSON or schema violation). **Spec amended** (§6.5 hardware para + agent table, §7 step 2): on a GPU-less host the local 9B is impractical, so chunking defaults to **cloud_free**; `local_small` is a config swap when a GPU is configured. **Deps:** `jinja2==3.1.6` added; `httpx==0.28.1` promoted to runtime. **54 tests pass** (agent against a mocked `LLMProvider`: happy path, retry-on-malformed-JSON/schema-violation/reversed/negative range, code-fence strip, give-up, PL/EN routing, injection-safety, tier selection; `OllamaProvider` via `httpx.MockTransport`: request shape, `format` omission, bearer auth, 5xx); ruff + mypy --strict + dep-age clean; `main` green. **Review:** own-review via the new `/review-pr` skill caught a jinja2-in-agent layering smell (fixed: `prompts` raises its own `PromptNotFound`); two Codex notes folded pre-merge — the prompt-injection redesign and the `paragraph_range` validator (upper-bound-vs-count deferred to Session 4 persistence). **Process (retro):** created `/review-pr` (PR #11, `d90ed76`) and wired it into CLAUDE.md's Merge flow. **Lesson:** I waved prompt-injection through as "inherent to the feature" in my own review; an external reviewer caught it — the fix (derive structure from the trusted template, never reparse user-rendered output) is now a `/review-pr` check and a saved memory.
- **2026-05-21 — Session 2 complete: story upload → validate → sandbox → parse → detect → persist (PR #8, squash `c692cba`).** `POST /stories/upload` (spec §7 step 1) accepts `.txt`/`.md`/`.docx`, validates (extension allowlist → 415, Content-Type with params stripped, 10 MiB cap → 413, empty/unparseable → 400), sandboxes the original (UUID-named, `0o700` dir / `0o600` file, no exec — §6.7, dir chmod explicit so it holds for a pre-existing dir), parses to raw text + paragraph blocks, detects PL/EN, and persists a `Project` (detected language) + `Story` (raw text). I/O-pure `domain/parsing.py` + `domain/language.py` (seeded `langdetect`); `adapters/{db,upload_storage}.py`; thin `api/stories.py` wired in `main.py`. New deps exact-pinned ≥14d, no advisories: `langdetect==1.0.9`, `python-docx==1.2.0`, `python-multipart==0.0.27`. **38 tests pass** (parser/detection/storage/db units + upload integration: happy txt→en & docx→pl, 415/413/400, sandbox write+perms, charset-param accept); ruff + mypy --strict + dep-age clean; `main` green (all four CI jobs). **Review:** two Codex notes folded in pre-merge — `libpq_kwargs` now preserves URL query options (sslmode/timeouts) and the route strips Content-Type parameters; own-review also de-duplicated `conftest`'s copy of `libpq_kwargs` and filed a cross-cutting note for orphaned-sandbox-file cleanup on upload failure (deferred, harmless single-user). **Process (retro):** encoded PR-first/`wrap-session`-last in the wrap skill (preflight step 0 + reframed step 8) and added a `backend/CLAUDE.md` test convention (bind secret-keyword values to a variable so detect-secrets doesn't flag them). **Lesson:** a happy-path test that hard-codes a clean `Content-Type` ("text/plain") hides the real-world parameterized form ("text/plain; charset=utf-8") — test the input the browser actually sends.
- **2026-05-21 — Issue #4 closed: both CVE-stale images fixed, `main` fully green (infra/governance, no M1 code).** pgvector `0.8.1-pg17-bookworm` → `0.8.2-pg17-trixie` (the pre-approved 7-day-rule bend for a CVE-fix release; trixie carries 9 OS CVEs vs bookworm's 13, and older is strictly worse — 0.8.1-trixie = 42). Fixing it unmasked a second stale image, ollama `0.22.1` (sequential-Trivy masking, the same pattern neo4j→pgvector showed in #2) → bumped to `0.24.0` (freshest aged stable, 7 days, no bend; dropped the CRITICAL + 6 others, 17 → 12 HIGH). Residual CVEs that no tag can fix are waived per-CVE in scoped `infra/trivy/{pgvector,ollama}.trivyignore` — pgvector's OS CVEs (no fresher rebuild) + bundled `gosu`/Go-stdlib, and ollama's compiled-in Go-stdlib + `buger/jsonparser` — each with a reachability assessment (none network-reachable on a 127.0.0.1 single-user non-root deployment: gnutls unused since Postgres TLS is OpenSSL, no DTLS, no systemd daemon; ollama CVEs are mostly DoS a trusted local caller self-inflicts, the two cert-validation ones need MITM of outbound TLS). Added `infra/trivy/WAIVERS.md`, a consolidated review register (every waived CVE across neo4j/pgvector/ollama with fixed-in versions + drop conditions) for periodic re-checking. Applied to `docker-compose.yml`, the CI backend `postgres` service container, the wrapper `infra/ollama/Dockerfile`, and both Trivy scan steps. pgvector waiver verified locally (dockerized Trivy → exit 0); ollama CVE list enumerated from the CI Trivy run. Squash-merged (PR #6, `4cb92a2`), Issue #4 closed. **Process (retro):** amended `/pin-image` — local-Trivy-unreadable → push-and-harvest-from-CI fallback; scan all images up front; record waivers in `WAIVERS.md`. **Lesson:** the sequential-Trivy unmask is now a confirmed *pattern*, not a one-off — fixing image N reveals staleness in image N+1, so sweep every image the security job scans before declaring it will go green. And in this environment local Trivy on large images is unusable (sandboxed background), so CI is the authoritative scanner.
- **2026-05-21 — Issue #2 fixed + image-pinning process hardened (infra/governance, no M1 code).** neo4j repointed from the nonexistent `5.26.25-community-bullseye` to `5.26.25-community-ubi10` in `docker-compose.yml` (neo4j + neo4j-init) and `ci.yml`; UBI-10 zeroes the 14 Debian OS CVEs, and the 3 bundled-netty HIGH CVEs are waived with per-CVE justification in `infra/trivy/neo4j.trivyignore` (scoped to the neo4j scan step).
